KA (425 ff.)
0. Dge idan snyan brgyud kyi gdams pa'i gter mdzod rje shes rab
rgya mtsho dpal bzang po'i gsung 'bum ka pa'i dkar chag
ff. 2
1. Zhabs brtan gsol 'debs kyi 'grel pa shes ldan dad pa'i chu
gter 'phel ba'i zla shel phreng ba
ff. 88
Margin: Rnam thar bstod 'grel Ka --
/ces 'dzam gling bstan pa'i nyi ma nges don chos kyi rgyal po
mkhas shing grub pa'i dbang phyug 7rdo rje 'chang shes rab
rgya mtsho d pal bzang po'i zhal snga nas kyi sku che ba'i yon
tan las brtsams te rang bzhin brjod pa'i rgyan gyi sgo nas
bstod cing gsol ba 'debs pa'i tshigs su bcad pa gsang bdag zla
ba bzang po mi yi gar gyis mam par rol pa 'jam mgon sde khri
rin po ches mdzad pa 'di la 'grel pa rgyas pa mnam thar dang
bcas pa zhig dgos zhes gsol 'debs de nyid bka' rtsom zhu ba po
bla ma rin po che'i phyag g.yog lo nyi shu rtsa grangs la thugs
zin nges ngal gso med par grub pa'i nye gnas rnam dpyod mchog
tu yangs pa dge slong byams pa rgya mtshos sa gsum na myed
par aka' ba'i rten mchog rje bla ma nyid kyi phyag sbyang gi
tshe sku rked du rgyun ring dkris pa'i sku gzan bub tshang/
bzhugs gdan khri snyan sa le'i pags pa'i tshal bu/ bkra shis
rtags kyis spras pa'i mdzod dar srid du ring ba bcas nan cher
bskul ba dang/ phyis su khri chen rab brtan rgya mtsho'i sprul
pa'i sku mkhyen rab kyi dbang phyug dam pa dkon mchog bstan
dzin rgya mtshos mam thar rgyas pa zhig nang du 'bri dgos
zhes kyang kha dar dang gsung phebs pa'i ngor/ rnam thar chen
mo phyis su 'byung ba la bsam nas gsol 'debs kyi tshig don
'grel pa gtso bor byas te/ rje btsun bla ma de nyid kyi zhabs
rdul spyi bos bsten pa'i bran gyi tha ma 7 btsun gzugs ngag
dbang thub bstan rgya mtshos myos ldan gyi lo (1879) 'i sa ga'i
yang tshes bzang por mjug grub par sbyar ba 'dis kyang 'gro kun
theg mchog gi bshes gnyen dam pas rjes su 'dzin cing/ 'jam
mgon bstan pa'i snying po dri ma med pa phyogs dus thams cad
du dar zhing rgyas par gyur cig/
2. Phags yul mkhas grub yongs kyi gtsug rgyan grub pa'i slob
dpon chen po mi tra dzo ki'i rtogs pa brjod pa zung 'jug grub
pa'i gtan snyan
ff. 3
Margin: Mi tra'i rtogs brjod Ka
/tshul 'di 'jam dbyangs bla ma'i gsung bzhin du/
bka' 'bangs bikşu pra dznyā să ga ras/
Zrmad byung rnam par thar pas yid drangs te
7dga' ldan chos 'khor gling du bris pa dge/
3. Rje'i bstod pa rtsa 'grel gyi bshad lung gi brjed byang thor
bu nor bu'i phra tshom
ff. 35
Margin: Rje'i bstod zin Ka
/ces 'jam mgon bla ma chos kyi rgyal po tsong kha pa chen po
de nyid slar yang gsum ldan ngur smrig 'chang ba'i rnam par
rol pa khri chen gung thang 'jam pa'i dbyangs di pam mtshan
can gyis mdzad pa'i legs bshad zla med pa rje'i bstod pa don
ldan rtsa 'grel gyi bshad lung smra ba'i dbang phyug 'jam

Shes-rab-rgya-mtsho
dbyangs bla ma khri chen rdo rje 'chang dkon mchog rgyal
mtshan pa'i drung nas legs par mnos pa'i tshe brjed byang
cung zad bkod pa la slar yang phri bsnan dang/ gsang bdag
sde khri rin po che 'jam dbyangs thub bstan nyi mas smon
lam gyi gsung chos la bstod 'grel gyi bshad pa gnang ba'i
skabs kyi zhal gdams mnams kyis kyang zur brgyan te] btsun
gzugs shes rab rgya mtshos sug bris su byas pa 'di yang
tshe rabs thams cad du 'jam mgon bla ma'i lugs bzang bshad
sgrub gnyis kyi sgo nas rang gzhan gyi rgyud la 'phel zhing
rgyas pa'i rgyu kho nar gyur cig/
Rten 'brel bstod pa rtsa'grel gyi bshad lung gi brjed byang
thub dbang dgyes pa'i mchod sprin
ff. 39
Margin: Rten bstod 'grel pa Ka
ces rten 'brel bstod pa rtsa 'grel las brtsams pa'i gtam 'di
yang mgon po mkhyen brtse'i gter chen 'jam dbyangs bla ma dkon
mchog rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i zhal nas ji ltar thos pa
bzhin/ btsun gzugs shes rab rgya mtshos rang nyid zab mo'i lam
la bag chags mthu brtas pa'i rgyur dmigs te dran tshod rags
rim tsam brjed thor btab pa'o/
5. Srad rgyud lugs kyi bla ma'i mal 'byor dga' ldan lha brgya
mar grags pa'i khrid kyi zin bris dngos grub nor bu'i snye ma
ff. 28
Margin: Dga' lha'i khrid zin Ka
ces srad rgyud lugs kyi bla ma'i mal 'byor dga' ldan lha
brgya mar grags pa'i khrid kyi zin bris dngos grub nor bu'i
snye ma zhes bya ba 'di yang 'jam dpal dbyangs dngos rje btsun
dkon mchog bstan pa'i sgron me dpal bzang podang/ 'jam dbyangs
bla ma rje dkon mchog rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i bka' drin
las lam 'di'i dmigs khrid zhib rgyas yang yang mnos pa dge
slong shes rab rgya mtshos dran tho tsam du yi ger bkod pa'o/
6. Srad rgyud lugs kyi bla ma'i rnal 'byor dga' ldan lha brgya
ma'i dmigs rim brjed byang du bkod pa zab lam nor bu'i gan
mdzod
ff. 16
Margin: Dga' khrid brjed byang Ka --
ces srad rgyud lugs kyi bia ma'i rnal 'byor dga' ldan lha
brgya ma'i khrid kyi dmigs rim brjed byang du bkod pa zab lam
nor bu'i gan mdzod ces bya ba 'di yang rgyal ba kun las lhag
pa'i bka' drin mtshungs pa ma mchis pa 'jam dbyangs bla ma
rdo rje 'chang dkon mchog rgyal mtshan d pal bzang po'i zhal
las slar yang khrid tshar gnyis thos pa bzhin/ dge slong shes
rab rgya mtshos rang gi dran pa'i gsal 'debs su bris palo/
Dga' idan lha brgya ma'i gzhung bsrangs kyi khrid kyi zin bris
ff. 13
Margin: Dga' lha'i khrid Ka
bzhi
/dga' ldan lha brgya ma'i gzhung bsrangs kyi bshad lung u cu
mu chin don grub kyis zhus ngor rab byung bcu gnyis pa'i bgrang
bya sum cu pa me sprel (1716) zla ba dang po'i tshes dgu la
btsal skabs/ spyir rang cag mnams kyis dal 'byor gyi rten bzang
rnam par dag pa thob/...
No colophon

byang grub gnyis dga' ston

Shes-raborgya-mtsho
/zhes mkhas grub chib brgyud kyi bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi brjed
byang 'di yang dmigs pa med pa'i thugs rje chen po dang ldan
pa bka' drin zla med 7'jam dbyangs bla ma dkon mchog rgyal
mtshan dpal bzang po dang/ smra ba'i dbang phyug 'jam dbyangs
bla ma dkon mchog dgyes pa'i blo gros rnam gnyis las 'di'i
nyams khrid legs par thob pa'i tshe dge slong shes rab rgya
mtshos dran gso tsam du bris pa'o/
9. Srad rgyud lugs kyi dga' ldan 'pho khrid kyi brjed byang mi
pham bla ma'i zhal lung
ff. 9
Margin: Dga' ldan 'pho khrid Ka --
dir srad rgyud lugs kyi dga' ldan 'pho khrid thun mong ma
History of
yin pa dmigs brtse ma 'bum gyi bka' rgya can gyi khrid snga
Dmigs brtse
phyir lan bzhi tsam mnos pa i skabs kyi brjed byang tho tsam
ma 'bum
bri bar bya'o/ /de'ang 'di'i khrid kun mkhyen 'jam dbyangs
bzhad pa'i rdo rje yan chad yi ge med pa'i snyan brgyud du
bzhugs pa las thugs sras 'jam dbyangs bde ba'i rdo rjes gsan
te zin bris tshig lhug dang/ dpai 'khor chos sde'i mkhan chen
klu 'bum dge 'dun rgya mtshos bskul nas khrid yig tshigs bcad
ma zhig dang gnyis mdzad pa'i snga ma'i lung dang/ phyi ma'i
khrid lung yong pas dga' idan lha brgya ma'i khrid thob nas
dmigs brtse ma sum 'bum mam 'bum song ba'am min kyang 'bum
'don pa'i dam bca' byas nas nyan dgos pa kho rang gi bka' rgya
yin sbyangs pa'i sngon du dmigs brtse ma 'bum ther gsum mam
gcig ma mtha' gtong/ de'ang grub chen nam mkha' rgyal mtshan
la gsang bdag gis byams mgon nyid la bslab btus zhus shig
gsungs pa'i phyi nyin rje bdag nyid chen po lho brag tu byon/
grab chen gyis byams mgon dngos su gzigs pas rje bla ma dang
byams mgon thugs rgyud gcig pa dang/ rje btsun 'jam dbyangs
sogs dang thugs rgyud gcig pa'ang chos sku dbyer med kyi klong
nas gzugs skur ston tshul mi 'dra ba'i khyad par red/...
/de dus gsang mtshan 'jam dbyangs bde ba'i rdo rje dang/ pha
bong kha pa 'jam dbyangs grags pa las bsnyen par rdzogs pa'i
mtshan blo bzang 'jam dpal rgya mtsho zhes yod par 'khrul nas
'ga' zhig gis rje 'dis mdzad pa'i dmigs brtse ma'i khrid yig
la rgyal ba 'jam dpal rgya mtshos mdzad pa zhes tho yig bris
pa mthong gsungs/
mkhar rdo bzod pa rgya mtsho/ rgyud chen rta mgrin phun
tshogs/ re bstan pa lhun grub/ yer pa phun tshogs rgya mtsho/
chu bar dge 'dun bkra shis/ gong dkar ba kun dga' mang thos
rgya mtsho/ se ra tā dbon pandi ta blo bzang sbyin pa/ khri
co ne ba blo bzang dar rgyas/ rmor chen kun dga' lhun grub/
klu 'bum chos rgya mtsho sogs sa dge'i mkhas pa brgya phrag
gi zhabs la gtugs/ sgo mang bla ma blo bzang shes rab las mi
tra dang/ bka' gyur ba blo bzang tshul khrims las rdor phreng
gsan nas khri ngag dbang mchog ldan dang/ mkhan chen dge 'dun
rgya mtsho sogs la gnang ba'i rgyun rgyal dbang bskal bzang
rgya mtsho dang/ pan chen dpal ldan ye shes kyis spel bas dus
phyis bar mdo dbus kun tu khyab che/ kun mkhyen 'jam dbyangs
bzhad pa dang/ thang sag pa dngos grub rgya mtsho mam gnyis
las dpal ldan srad rgyud kyi gdams pa rdzogs par mnos nas gsung
rgyun mi nyams pa'i phyir bka' rtsom yang pot chen gcig yod/
rgyal ba bskal bzang rgya mtsho sngar 'grel pa bzhi sbrags
gnang skabs dka' gnad (f. 8v) kyi dri ba'i lan rgyud pa mkhan po
brgyud de thogs med du phul ba dang/ cun gar dus gzhung sa nas
rim gro gnang bar nang du bud med gos dmar po gyon pa zhig
'gro ba'i phyi bzhin song bar su yang mi 'dug/ sa gzhi ri dang
bcas pa ldem ldem giyos pas rtsar gcod ma nus par bzhag ces
bsod grags rdo rje 'chang gis gsungs/
bud med de yi dam gyi mam 'phrul du gsungs/ glang ra'i

Shes-rab-rgya-mtsho
/cho ga 'di sde khri rang gi gsung ji bzhin tshang ba
bkod thog/ gong gi lha'i mngon rtogs skabs phyag mtshan gyi
yig chung mnams 7rgyal mchog skal bzang rgya mtsho'i gsung
gi thugs dkyil 'don chog nas tshur kha bskangs pa yin pas/
rjes sor cho ga 'don pa rams nas lha'i mngon rtogs cung
rgyas par spro skabs mngon rtogs yig chen yig chung dkyus
gcig tu sbrel nas 'don pa dang/ bsdus pa'i skabs phyag mtshan
gyi yig chung mams dor nas yig chen rkyang pa bton chog pas
yig chung la zhib tu brtags nas so so'i 'dor len gyi khyad
par phyed par mdzad dgos so/
14. Dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i bskyed rim gyi mam bzhag 'jam dpal
zhal lung
ff. 79
Margin: Dus bskyed Ka --
ces bcom ldan das dus kyi 'khor lo'i bskyed rim gyi mam
bzhag gsal bar bshad pa 'jam dpal grags pa'i dpal gyi zhal
lung zhes bya ba 'di ni/ sde snod 'dzin pa sman pa slob zur
tshul khrims rgya mtsho nas 'di'i bskyed rim gyi mam bzhag
sngar yod 'ga' zhig rgyas drag pas blo dman gyis 'chun dka'
zhing/ la la bsdus drag pas rdzogs par go mi nus par 'dug
pas/ go bde zhing rgyas bsdus 'tshams pa zhig gyis zhes khong
rang shambha la'i zhing du smon lam 'debs pa'i rten du yang
yang bskul ba'i ngor 'jam dbyangs chos kyi rgyal po dkon mchog
jigs med dbang po'i zhal snga nas dang/ ngon de'i thugs kyi
sras po 'jam pa'i dbyangs dkon mchog bstan pa'i sgron me dpal
bzang po'i zhal snga nas sogs dam pa du ma'i zhabs rdul spyi
bor brten pa'i/ 7 shākya'i btsun pa 'jam dbyangs thub bstan
nyi mas chos grwa chen po bkra shis 'khyil gyi bskal bzang
mam 'dren rgyal ba'i pho brang gi nye dabs rang gshag e
wam dga' 'khyil du phal chen grub par bgyis shing mjug ngon
khang srid gsum mam rgyal du rdzogs par sbyar ba'i yig ge
pa ni su nyid dge slong 'jam dbyangs shes rab kyis bgyis pa
'dis kyang dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i bshad sgrub gnyis kyi
bstan pa rin po che/ sgo thams cad nas phyogs thams cad dar
zhing rgyas la yun ring du gnas par gyur cig/
/rgyal bstan spyi dang 'jam mgon bshad sgrub mtshor/ /skal
bzang ngang mo 'bum gyis rtsen pa'i slad /gnam bskos dga' ba
rgya Idan pho brang nas/ /'dzad med chos sbyin ganggā'i rgyun
'di spel/...
15. Bcom ldan 'das dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i zhi ba'i sbyin sreg gi
cho ga gsal bar bshad pa 'jam dbyangs dgongs rgyan
ff. 29
Margin: Dus sbyin Ka
/ces bcom ldan 'das dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i zhi ba'i sbyin
sreg gi cho ga gsal bar bshad pa jam dbyangs dgongs rgyan zhes
bya ba 'di ni rab byung bcu bzhi pa'i thog ma me yos lor (1807)
or du su o thog shog nas mam dpyod yangs pa rabbyams pa
blo bzang yon tan dang/ rang gi slob bu dpyod idan ku shri
'jigs med snyan grags sogs don gnyer can du mas snga phyir
bskul zhing/ nye char dad gtong sogs bsod nams kyi stobs
phun sum tshogs pa a ru hor chen bẽ li do rje pha lam dang/
chos tshul la mkhyen diyod kyi rtsal phun sum tshogs pa zhabs
drung blo bzang bstan 'phel nas dus 'khor gyi grwa tshang zhig
gsar du 'dzug dgos kyi rting bskul byung bstun rang nyid lam
'di la mchog tu mos pas kyang mtshams sbyar te sa 'brug gi
lo (1808) nas 'go brtsams te sku gsung thugs yongs rdzogs
kyi bsgrub mchod sbyin sreg dang bcas pa bshad sgrub bstan
pa'i 'byung gnas chos grwa chen po bkra shis 'khyil gyi phyag
len ji ita ba bzhin btsugs skabs/ sbyin sreg gi cho ga gsar
bsgrigs 'di lta bu zhig dgos tshul gyi bskul ma byung bar

Shes-raborgya-mtsho
brten/ dus gsum sangs rgyas thams cad las kyang bka' drin
lhag par che ba/ 7rje btsun dam pa 'jam dbyangs chos kyi
rgyal po dkon mchog 'jigs med dbang po'i zhal snga nas kyi sku
'phreng snga phyi yab sras rnams kyi gsung gi bdud rtsi snying,
gi bum par thob cing, lam 'di la mchog tu mos pa dang ldan pa/
7 shākya'i dge slong jam dbyangs thub bstan nyi mas rang lo
so gcig par a mu hor chen be li'i dgon pa bkra shis chos 'khor
gling du cho 'phrul zla ba'i yar tshes dge bar sbyar ba'i yi
ge pa ni dad brtson blo dang dan pa dge tshul ngag dbang blo
bzang ngo/.
16. Bcom ldan 'das dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i thugs dkyil gyi sgo nas
bsnyen pa bya tshul dngos grub mam gnyis 'gugs pa'i lcags kyu
Margin: Bsnyen yig Ka
ff. 14
zhes dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i thugs dkyil gyi bsnyen pa ji
ltar bya tshul 'di ni/ gzhung sa mchog nas dus 'khor gyi bsnyen
pa bya 'dod pa mnams la phan phyir sde khri'i gsung dus 'khor
gyi bskyed rim dang/ thugs akyil 'don chog bsdus pa/ sbyin
sreg bcas rje shes rab rgya mtsho'i gsung 'bum dang chabs cig
par bskrun mdzad skabs/ bsnyen yig kha gsal 'khyer bde zhig
rung du snang yang/ sde khri'i gsung gi thugs dkyil bsnyen
yig ha cang bsdus drag cing/ sku 'bum che shos tshang gi gsung
bsnyen yig zhal gsal yang dus 'khor lha bcu gsum ma'i bsnyen
pa bya tshul gtso bor gsung 'dug stabs/ da lam bsnyen pa'i
mnam bzhag byings rnams che shos gsung nyid gzhi bzhag thog/
dngos gzhi cho ga'i skor lha bcu gsum ma'i sgos chos mams
dor nas/ sde khri'i gsung gi bsnyen yig Itar bkod de/ thugs
dkyil gyi bsnyen pa bya 'dod pa mnams kyis 'khyer bde'i luge
su phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa lags so/
See: Dkar chag: /dus 'khor skor le tshan 'di bzhi sde khri'i gsung
nas nyer mkhor gsar bcug go/
KHA (425 ff)
0. Dge idan snyan brgyud kyi gdams pa'i gter mdzod rje shes rab
rgya mtsho dpal bzang po'i gsung 'bum kha pa'i dkar chag
ff. 2
1. 'Dus pa 'phags lugs lha so gnyis pa'i lam rim pa dang po'i khrid
dmigs kyi brjed byang mi bskyod mgon po'i zhal lung
ff. 102
Margin: Gsang bskyed Kha -
/ces 'dus pa'i lam rim pa dang po'i brjed byang mi bskyod mgon
po'i zhal lung zhes bya ba 'di yang dus gsum gyi rgyal ba thams
cad las kyang nges par thugs rje dang bka' drin mtshungs zla ma
mchis pa snyan brgyud rgya mtsho'i mnga' bdag dpal ldan bla ma
dam pa mtshan brjod par dka' ba/ 7rje btsun dkon mchog rgyal
mtshan dpal bzang po'i bka' drin las rim gnyis kyi khrid mnos
pa'i skabs brjed tho cung zad bris pa de bzhin yi ger 'khod
pa dgos pa'i bskul ma 'debs mkhan mang du byung yang bdag 'dra
thun mong ba'i lam gyi sne zin tsam la yang blo sbyangs ma song
ba'i gang zag gis snyan brgyud kyi gdams pa 'di 'dra 'god pa
la skrag pas bzhag kyang/ nye char thugs rje bdag nyid bla ma
yab sras rnams kyis bris chog pa'i bka'i gnang ba stsal ba mi
bskyod mgon po rang gi gsung dang dbyer ma mchis pa'i byin
rlabs kho na la brten nas/ dge slong shes rab rgya mtshos zin
tho snga phyi phyogs bsdebs su byas pa la rang nyid sbyangs pa
zhan pa'i bio skyon gyis sbags pa dang/ zhal shes kyi rigs gsal
bar bris pa sog's nongs pa mtha' dag bla ma lhag pa'i lha bka'

Shes-rab-rgya-mtsho
sdod dang bcas pa la snying nas 'chags shing/ dge bas tshe
rabs thams cad du bla ma lhas rjes su bzung ste tshe la ma
nor ba'i lam bzang po 'di spyod pa'i snod idan du gyur nas/
phyogs bcu'i zhing khams rab 'byams su rgyal ba kun gyi dam
chos ma lus pa rgyal ba'i dgongs pa bzhin du 'dzin nus par
gyur cig/ /mangga lam/
2. Dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i rdzogs rim rim lnga'i amar khrid kyi
brjed byang mi bskyod zhal gyi bdud rtsi
ff. 39
Margin: Gsang rdzogs Kha --
ces dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i rdzogs rim rim lnga'i dmar khrid
kyi brjed byang mi bskyod zhal gyi bdud rtsi zhes bya ba 'di
yang/ rim gnyis kyi gdams pa'i bang md zod 'dzin pa zla bral
smra ba'i dbang phyug/ 7rje btsun thams cad mkhyen pa dkon
mchog rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i bka' drin las 'di'i nyams
khrid thob pa'i skabs brjed tho cung zad bris pa la/ phyis
su bla ma rdo rje 'chang yab sras rnams kyis de bzhin yi ger
bkod chog pa'i bka'i gnang ba spyi bor stsal ba'i byin rlabs
kho na la brten nas/ dge slong shes rab rgya mtshos zin tho
snga phyi rnams phyogs bsdebs su byas pa la rang gi blo skyon
gis sbags pa dang/ zhal shes mams gsal bar bkod pa sogs kyis
lam la sgrib par mi 'gyur zhing/ tshe rabs thams cad du bla
ma lhag pa'i Ihas brtse bas rjes su bzung ste/ dpa' bo dang
mal 'byor ma'i dbang phyug bye ba brgya phrag gang nas gshegs
pa'i lam bzang 'di dang skad cig tsam yang mi 'brał zhing/
bstan pa'i snying po dri ma med pa bshad sgrub zung gis sgo
nas phyogs dus kun tu rgyas par byed nus par gyur cig/ /mangga
lam/
3. 'Dus pa'i rtsa rgyud kyi gleng gzhi sbas bshad kyi yi ge bzhi
bcu'i gsal byed rdo rje'i lam gyi sgron me
ff. 3
Margin: Gsang rgyud sbas bshad Kha --
/'ai la yi ge mang ba bzhi bcu dang/ nyung ba so bdun du byas
pa'i phyogs gnyis dang/ 'chad tshul la mngon shes can nam brtson
grus bzang pos gzhung gong og ma dkrigs pa dang/ btsun mo can
dang bod phal cher gyis gzhung gong 'og drugs nas 'chad tshul
gnyis rdor phreng gi dgongs pa bzhin rje 'gos sogs kyis yi ge
bsnan pa dang/ skal ldan grags pa dang thugs rje dpal zhabs
gnyis kyis yi ge ma bsnan par chad pa'i lugs yod do/
7mtshan tsam gyis kyang byang chub rdo rje'i go 'phang sgrub
byed 'dus pa'i rtsa rgyud kyid /gleng gzhi sbas bshad yi ge
bzhi bcu'i gsal byed nyung ngu rdo rje'i lam sgron 'di/ /rje
btsun mi bskyod mgon po'i drin las btsun gzugs shes rab rgya
mtshos bkod pa'i dges) /rmad byung lam 'dis gro kun sgrol ba'i
rin chen lta bu'i gdul byar bdag gyur cig/ /mangga lam?
Grub chen lū i pa'i lugs kyi dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i bskyed
rim he ru ka'i zhal lung
ff. 71
Margin: Bde bskyed Kha -
/ces grub chen lū i pa'i lugs kyi dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i rim
pa dang po'i khrid kyi gsal byed he mu ka'i zhal lung zhes bya
ba 'di yang sku bzhi'i bdag nyid khyab bdag 'khor lo'i mgon po
7 rdo rje chang dkon mchog rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i zhabs
drung nas khrid zhib rgyas lan du mar thob pa'i skabs kyi gsung
bshad mams phyogs bsgrigs su byas chog par bla ma yab sras kyi
bka'i gnang ba thob pa bzhin/ gdams ngag skal ma nyam (=?mnyam)
du nod pa'i chos mthun gyi grogs du ma'i gsung gis yang yang
bskul ba'i thugs bzhed bskang ba dang/ gtso cher rang nyid
rmongs rtul dang brjed nges kyi dbang du song ba'i dran gsor

Shes-rab-rgya-mtsho
dmigs nas dge slong shes rab rgya mtshos bshad sgrub bstan
pa'i 'byung gnas dpal ldan bkra shis 'khyil gyi chos grwar
dbu brtsams te/ mjug sman lung bkra shis chos 'phel gling
du rdzogs par bgyis pa'o/ /sarba mangga lam/
5. Grub mchog lũ i pa'i lugs kyi dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i rdzogs
rim mal byor chen po'i dmar khrid he ma ka'i zhal gyi bdud
rtsi
ff. 28
Margin: La rdzogs Kha --
/ces grub mchog lū i pa'i lugs kyi dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i
rdzogs rim rnal 'byor chen po'i dmar khrid he ru ka'i zhal
gyi bdud rtsi zhes bya ba 'di yang khyab bdag he ru ka dpal
ngur smrig 'chang ba'i mam par rol pa zla med rje btsun
dam pa yab sras gsum gyis yi ger 'god pa'i bka'i gnang ba
stsal ba'i byin rlabs kho na la brten nas/ btsun gzugs shes
rab rgya mtshos dus gsum gyi rgyal ba thams cad las kyang
bka' drin dang thugs rje mtshungs pa ma mchis pa 'jam mgon
smra ba'i dbang phyug rdo rje 'chang dngos 7ratna dhwa dza'i
zhal snga nas las snga phyir khrid rgyas bsdus lan mang du
mnos pa'i skabs kyi gsung bshad blo dang rtsol bas gang lcogs
gung bsgrigs te phyogs bsdebs su byas pa 'di yang tshe rabs
thams cad du mgon po mchog des 'bral med dgyes bzhin rjes su
bzung ste sku gsung thugs kyi gsang ba ma lus pa 'dzin pa'i
sras kyi thu bor gyur te/ nam mkha' ji srid gnas kyi bar du
rgyal ba sras bcas kyi spyod pa dang smon lam ma lus pa la
zhum pa med par slob pa'i snying stobs rgya mtsho'i riabs bzhin
dus las yol ba med par gong nas gong du 'phel ba'i rgyu kho
nar gyur cig/ /sarba mangga lam/
Bde mchog bskyed rim 'dod 'jo dang rdzogs rim dngos grub snye
ma'i bsdus don
ff. 4
Margin: Bde khrid sa bcad Kha --
/zhes bde mchog bskyed rim 'dod 'jo dang/ rdzogs rim angos
grub snye ma'i bsdus don 'di yang/ btsun gzugs shes rab rgya
mtshos gzhung gi khog cha blo ngor 'char skyen pa'i thabs su
bsam nas zur du bkol ba'o/
'Jam dpal dus dgra'i dbang po ma he'i gdong can bcu gsum lha'i
'khor lo'i rim pa dang po i zab khrid zin bris 'jigs mdzad rdo
rje'i zhal lung
ff. 68
Margin: 'Jigs bskyed Kha --
/ceš 'jam dpal dus dgra'i dbang po ma he'i gdong can bcu gsum
lha'i 'khor lo'i rim pa dang po'i zab khrid zin bris jigs
mdzad rdo rje'i zhal lung zhes bya ba 'di yang/ sangs rgyas kun
'dus kyi ngo bo kun mkhyen 'jam dbyangs bzhad pa'i rdo rje 7rje
btsun blo bzang thub bstan 'jigs med rgya mtsho yab sras kyi
zhabs pad gtsug gis mchod pa'i bka' drin las lam 'di'i smin
byed kyi dbang/ grol byed rim gnyis kyi khrid/ rgyab rten gyi
lung/ rgyud kyi bshad pa las tshogs dang bcas man ngag gi bdud
rtsi tshim par myang ba dge slong shes rab rgya mtshos rang gi
brjed byang dang/ don du gnyer ba du mas yang yang bskul ngor
bris pa bla ma yi dam bka' sdod srung ma'i tshogs kyis bzod par
mdzad du gsol/
8. 'Jam dpal rdo rje bcu gsum lha'i 'khor lo'i rdzogs rim mal
'byor bzhi'i khrid kyi brjed byang 'jigs mdzad zhal gyi bdud rtsi
ff. 26
Margin: 'Jigs rdzogs Kha -
ces 'jam dpal rdo rje bcu gsum lha'i 'khor lo'i rdzogs rim mal
'byor bzhi'i khrid kyi brjed byang 'jigs mdzad zhal gyi bdud rtsi

Shes-rab-rgya-mtsho
zhes bya ba 'di yang mdo sngags kyi gsung rab mtha' dag la mi
jigs pa'i spobs pa brnyes nas gcig tu rgyal bstan spel ba'i
khur 'khyer bas mi ngal zhing snyan brgyud gdams pa'i bang
mdzod 'dzin pa smra ba'i dbang phyug rdo rje 'chang dkon mchog
rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i bka' drin las 'di'i rgyud dang
bskyed rdzogs chen mo'i bshad lung/ lam rim gnyis kyi dmar
khrid bcas yang yang mnos pa dge slong shes rab rgya mtshos
tho tsam brjed byang du byas pa bla ma mchog dang bka' sdod
srung ma'i tshogs kyis bzod par mdzad nas dgyes pa'i gar gyis
phyi nang gsang ba'i bdud sde'i g.yul las rgyal bar mdzad du
gsol/ /sarba mangga lam/
9. Bcom ldan 'das 'jigs mdzad rdo rje dpa' bo gcig pa la brten
pa'i zhi khro sbrags sgrub kyi gdams pa'i gsal byed shes rab
ral gri'i 'od zer 'bum 'gyed
ff. §
Margin: Zhi khro Kha --
/ces bcom ldan 'das 'jigs mdzad rdo rje dpa' bo gcig pa la
brten pa'i zhi khro sbrags sgrub kyi gdams pa'i gsal byed
shes rab ral gri'i 'od zer 'bum 'gyed ces bya ba 'di ni/ snyan
brgyud rgya mtsho'i mnga' bdag khyab bdag rdo rje sems dpa'i
ngo bo rje btsun bla ma dam pa dkon mchog rgyal mtshan dpal
bzang po'i zhal snga nas las man ngag gi bdud rtsi yang yang
thob pa'i snyoms las pa shes rab rgya mtshos zin thor btab
ste/ rje bla ma rang gi spyan lam du phab ste zhus dag bgyis
pa tshe rabs thams cad du zab gsal myur ba'i shes rab khyad
par can thob pa'i rgyur cig/ /bka' srung ye shes kyi spyan
idan mnams kyis kyang bla ma'i bka' bzhin chos 'di snod min
gyi lag tu mi gtong ba'i grogs mdzod cig/
10. Dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed dpa' bo gcig pa la brten nas chos rab
tu mnam 'byed kyi shes rab sgrub pa'i man ngag rdo rje'i tshig
gi mdud 'grol
ff. 5
Margin: Sbrags sgrub Kha --
.../'dir rgyal ba kun gyi yab gcig rje btsun 'jam dpal dbyangs
kyis khams gsum chos kyi rgyal po tsong kha pa chen po la
dngos su stsal ba'i gdams pa 'jam dbyangs phyi nang gsang gsum
dang/ rdo rje 'jigs byed dpa' bo gcig pa'i sku gsung thugs dus
gcig la bsrags nas sgrub pa'i man ngag nyung bsdus chog bsgrigs
ita bu'i nyams su blang bder 'god pa la/ de yang gzhung gi
dkyus ltar 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa dang sbrags kyang chog
mod/ 'on kyang 'jam dbyangs a ra pa tsa na am 'gro ba smin byed
ni 'jam dbyangs thams cad kyi sprul gzhi mes po Ita bu dang/
rtsod pa'i shes rab sgrub pa la bsngags pas 'di nyid lhag pa'i
lhar bsten na rten 'brel gyi gnad che bar rje bdag nyid chen
pos gsungs shing/ rdo rje'i tshig sbram du'ang 'byung ba bzhin
de dang sbrags dod na/ rgyu rdo rje 'dzin pa i skabs su bsgyur
kyang chog pas de lta na 'bras bu rdo rje 'dzin pa 'jam dpal gyi
zhal la'ang de'i nga rgyal 'dzin dgos/ ye shes (f. lv) sems dpa'i
skabs su bsgyur kyang chog/....
ces d pal rdo rje 'jigs byed dpa' bo gcig pa la brten nas chos
rab tu mam 'byed kyi shes rab sgrub pa'i man ngag rdo rje'i
tshig gi mdud 'grol zhes bya ba 'di yang thub bstan gsal ba'i
sgron me nyang tshang hu thog thu'i sprul pa'i sku rin po che
dkon mchog tshul khrims dang co ne mdo'i dkon gnyer dkon mchog
sbyin pa'am dpal ldan rgya mtsho rnam gnyis nas chog bsgrigs Ita
buli gshar sbyangs byed bde la zhal shes mams thon pa zhig dgos
zhes yang yang nan gyis bskul ngor/ btsun gzugs shes rab rgya
mtshos rang gi yid la goms pa'i slad du chos sde chen po d pal
ldan bkra shis 'khyil gi rang gshag nas sug bris su bgyis pa'o



Shes-rab-rgya-mtsho
11
11. 'Jam dbyangs chos skor gyi rjes gnang khrid dang bcas pa'i
brjed byang thugs rje nyin byed 'od kyis phye ba'i dad pa'i
padmo'i 'dzum zer
Pf. 9
Margin: 'Jam chos Kha --
/zhes dpa' bo rdo rje'i 'jam dbyangs chos skor gyi rjes
gnang khrid dang bcas pa'i brjed byang thugs rje i nyin byed
Tod kyis phye ba'i dad pa'i padmo'i 'dzum zer zhes bya ba
'di yang/ rje btsun bla ma de nyid kyi zhabs pad yun ring
bsten pa'i dge slong shes rab rgya mtshos man ngag lhan cig
thob pa'i grogs dag gi dran gso dang/ bla ma'i gsung rgyun
dus kyi mthar yang mi nyams par smon pa'i yid kyis bskui te
bris pa'o/
12. 'Jam dpal zhi drag gi bsrung ba'i gdams pa sra brtan rdo rje'i
go cha

nams mtshan can khrir bzhugs dus smon lam gyi nyin kha shas
la sku 'khrugs shig gi dbang gis phebs ma thub pa'i rkyen
gyis 'jam dpal dbyangs dngos sde khri rin po che 7rje btsun

phebs pa'i skabs kyi nyin so so'i gsung bshad rje thams cad
mkhyen pa pradznyà sā ga ras zin bris mdzad pa nyid kyi phyag
bris ngo ma las bshus pa'o/

bris, su byas pa

shes rab rgya mtshos bris/

pa'o/

ff. 1

pa'i chu thigs
ff. 513
Margin: Gsan yig Cha --
/ces zab rgyas dam pa'i chos kyi thob yig bdud rtsi'i chu
rgyun zhes bya ba 'di yang dus gsum gyi rgyal ba thams cad las
kyang thugs rje dang bka' drin zla med pa'i drin can bla ma
dam pa rnams las chos kyi bgo skal thob pa rnams bya lam
rjes med du mi 'gro ba'i phyir brjed tho re bris pa la phyis
su bstan la gcig tu dgongs pa'i lhag bsam gyi zla ba nya gang
ba'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen mang pos bskul zhing/ la las bri
shog sogs kyi rkyen sbyar ba la brten nas slar bla ma rdo rje
'chang chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i zhal
snga nas kyis bka' chos rgyun akon pa'i rigs gzhan las nyan
rgyu dang/ brgyud yig gsal kha thon pa bris shig ces gsung
bkod gnang yod pas bka' bzhin sgrub pa'i mchod par dmigs nas
btsun gzugs shes rab rgya mtshos rang lo don gsum pa shing.
phag (1875; b. 1803) lo rgyu skar gyi bdag po nag pa'i dga'
mas yongs su nya ba'i dkar phyogs kyi rgyal ba gsum par rang
nyid kyis sug bris su re zhig rdzogs par bgyis pa phyogs dus
kun tu bshad pa dang sgrub pa'i bstan pa dbyar mtsho ltar 'phel
zhing rgyas pa'i rgyu kho nar gyur cig]

bdud rtsi'i chu rgyun.

/de ltar mkhas grub chen po rje shes rab rgya mtsho'i gsung
bum 'di nyid nyams len la gzhol ba mnams la nyer mkho rmad
du byung ba bzhugs kyang dbus 'dir dpe rgyun dkon par brten

pa'o/

1. 'Dul ba mdo rtsa'i brjed byang thor bu blang dor mam 'byed
ff. 40
Margin: Mdo rtsa'i khrid zin Ja
/ces 'dul ba mdo rtsa'i brjed byang thor bu blang dor mam
byed ces bya ba 'di yang rmad byung thos bsam gling gi dka'
rams 'dzin gra nas sgo mang đpon slob ngag dbang dge legs
kyi sprul pa'i sku mkhyen rab kyi dbang phyug dam pa ngag
dbang thub bstan rgya mtshos dus 'khor bsdus rgyud kyi dpe
khyad 'phags dang/ skyor d pon rab brgyan rgya mtsho sogs slob
gnyer ba thams cad kyis lha rdzas bcas zin bris shig gyis
zhes bskul zhing/ de nas bgrang bya lnga pa shing mo glang
(1865) gu shri blo bzang tshephel gyi sprul sku rdo rams
pa 'jam dbyangs bstan'dzin rgya mtsho dang/ skyor dpon chos
'byor rgya mtsho sogs tshang mas thugs khur bzhes te yang
bskyar mdzod btags dang bcas rting bskul nan tan mdzad pas dge
'dun gyi sdes chos ldan gyi bsgo pa rnal gzon du mi rung ba
dang/ mang mang la chos bka' gnang ba'i tha ma'i zhal chem
lta bur snang ba dang/ rang gis kyang bla mas gsungs pa tshig
'bru re yin kyang brjed pas chud za bar phangs te/ btsun
gzugs shes rab rgya mtshos blo gros dang spob pas gang lcogs
tsam zhig gong og gi mtshams 'byed sla ba'i phyir rdzogs tshig
re smos pa ma gtogs phal cher gsung ris ma nyams pa'i tshul
du bris pa 'di yang...
2. Bstan bcos mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan gyi tshig gis mtshams
rnam par brgyan pa gzhong don ita ba'i mig 'byed

Margin: Mngon rgyan sa bcad Ja --

Art
Rie bdag nyid chen po sogs kyi sku brnyan 'ga' zhig gi 10 rgyus
cung zad briod pa mnyan par 'os pa'i gtam gvi phreng ba
Author: A-khu-ching Shes-rab-rgya-mtsho, 1803-1875.
Vol. Ka of the Lhasa Zhol New Printery edition of the Gsung-'bum.
ff. 12
na mo su ma ti kirti ye/
zung 'jug sgyu ma'i sku la dbang 'byor bas/
sku gsung thugs rten brtan g.yo rab 'byams su/
mos pa'i mtha' bzhin 'gog med rtag 'char ba/
/'jam dpal snying pos byang chub bar du skyongs/
f'dir rang gis mthong thos su gyur pa'i sku brnyan byin can
'ga' zhig gi 10 rgyus mdo tsam 'god pa la/ de yang khams gsum chos
kyi rgyal po 'jam mgon bla ma tsong kha pa chen po dgung lo nga
dgu bzhes pa'i shing lug (1415) la mi dbang grags pa rgyal mtshan
pas spyan drangs te 'dul 'dzin grags pa rgyal mtshan sogs 'khor
sde snod 'azin pa nyis brgya lhag tsam dang bcas 'on gyi bkra shis
do khar byon nas dbyar gnas mdzad/ yid bzang rtse pa mgos lo gzhon
nu dpal/ pan chen byams pa gling, pa bsod nams ram rgyal/ chos
rje gung snang ba mdzes pa dpal/ chos rje mi nyag rin rgyal ba/
rgod phrug grags pa 'byung gnas sogs mi chen dang/ ston chen bsam
gyis mi khyab pa 'dus/
a nyer gnyis rin po che spyan snga bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyis
nā ro chos drug gi khrid zhus te thabs lam tshigs bcad ma'i steng
nas gnang ba la yid bzang rtse pas zin bris mdzad/ rje dge 'dun
grub kyang 'di dus mjal te tshad ma'i dka' gnas gsung ba la zin.
bris yod/ byams pa gling pas chos khri'i logs la rje'i sku 'dra
lam rim brgyud pas bskor ba phyag bris mdzad (f. lv)
BKRA SHIS DO KHA MAr grags pa i sku brnyan byin can yang de Bkra-shis-
dus byung zhes mam thar las 'byung/ ngag rgyun la de dus rje
do-kha-ma
rin po ches nyin gcig la dbu skra sor phyed do ba brgyad bregs
pa'i tshul mdzad pa la/ sras kyi thu bo rdzu 'phrul la dbang 'byor
ba zhig gis sku bryan brgyad bzhengs pa'i gzungs gzhug la rje'i
dbu skra bubs tshang re bzhugs par gleng/ de yang sprul pa'i bzo
bos bzhengs pa dang/ 'ga' zhig gis mkhas grub rin po ches bzhengs
zer/
mkhas grub rje ni dgung lo lnga bcu pa me khyi'i lor (1406)
se ra chos sdings su mjal bas 'di dus 'khor du bzhugs yod med
dpyad/ pan chen blo bzang chos rgyan gyis bkra shis lhun po'i
phyi'i mchod rten gyi dkar chag tu/
bkra shis do kha mar grags chos kyi rje/
byams pa gling pa'i phyąg bzo las byung ba/,
/rje btsun bla ma'i sku 'dra byin rlabs can/ /zhes gsungs pa
dang/ khri stag lung brag pa blo gros rgya mtshos grub chen chos
pa rin po cher gnang ba'i rjeli sku pan chen byams pa gling pa'i
phyag bzo/ rje'i dbu skra bubs gcig gzungs su bzhugs pa la rje
rang gi phyag gis me tog 'thor ba yod ces rje skal idan rgya mtsho'i
rnam thar las 'byung ba ltar na paſ chen byams pa gling pa'i phyag
bzo yin pa 'dra/ gang ltar rje tsong kha pa'i sku bryan BKRA SHIS
GDONG KHA MA'am zur chag pas BKRA SHIS DO KHA MA brgyad kyi nang
tshan rgyal ba dge 'dun rgya mtsho'i (f. 2r) thugs dam rten sde pa
lha rgya ri ba nas rim par brgyud de 'ong ba'i lo rgyus kha byang
zhabs su bris yod pa zhig sngar bkra shis 'khyil rigs grwa'i rten
mjal gras su bzhugs kyang phyis blang ba gcig/
gzhan po ta la'i bla ma lha khang gi rten gtsor bkra shis do
kha ma gcig/
rgyal abang bskal bzang rgya mtsho'i sku gdung mchod rten gyi
bum pa'i gzungs gzhug tu rgyal ba na rim gyis thugs dam rten rje
bkra shis do kha ma byin rlabs kyi gzi 'od 'bar ba gcig/ de'i phyis
su pan chen dpal ldan ye shes kyis rgyal dbang 'jam dpal rgya mtshor
lam rim chen mo'i bshad lung phul ba'i mjug sems bskyed mchod pa'i

A-khu-ching on Art
skabs kyang rgyal ba'i thugs dam rten bkra shis do kha ma spyan
drangs par gsungs/ dga' ldan byang rtse'i gzims khang du gcig/
bya khyung dgon par khri ngag abang snyan grags pas bzhengs
pa'i sku'i gzungs gzhug tu rje de nyid kyi khu bo khri ngag dbang
chos grags pa'i thugs dam rten bkra shis do kha ma gcig/
gser khog btsan po'i bla brang gi rten khrod du rje bkra
shis do kha ma gcig/
bra sti sgrol ma gsung byon ma'i lha khang du'ang rje bkra
shis do kha ma sogs rten sna stong bzhugs zhes thos/
RJE NGA 'DRA MA ni rgyal ba tsong kha pa chen po zhal bzhugs Rje-nga-
pa'i dus su 'dra sku bdun bzhengs pa la byin rlabs kyi me tog rje 'ara-ma
rang nyid nas 'thor te nga dang 'dra zhes gsungs pas nga 'dra mar
grags/ de'i nang tshan goig dga' ldan har gdong gi rten gtsor
bzhugs pa jun wang ngag dbang dar rgyas kyis gzhung la zhus nas
gnang ba 'du khang steng gi shar gyi mchod khang dang po bka'
gdams lha khang du bzhugs pa 'di yin/ slar (f. 2v) yang sku
tshab bzhengs pa'i thebs su dngul rta rmig ma drug phul zer/ sku
dngos la rtse khru gang dang/ padma nyis rim la mkhyud gang
tsam/ rgyu sman 'dam las grub pa/ gong ba mthu bzlog/ dbu pan
dang pad sdong med/ phyag gnyis thugs kar chos 'khor mdzad cing/
zhabs phyed skyil gyis bzhugs pa zhig yod/
'ol kha chos bzang na rje'i dbu skra bubs gzungs su bzhugs
pa'i nga 'dra ma gcig/
Hol kha chos lung gi rten gtso rje dge legs rgya mtsho'i
phyag bzo yin zer ba'i rje'i sku nga 'dra ma gcig/
lha sa'i jo bo'i mtha' skor gyi mchod khang Inga par rje
nga 'dra ma gcig/
gzhan 'ol kha bsam gtan gling gi steng ngos rje'i sgrub khang
du rje zhal bzhugs dus mkhas grub rje'i phyag bzo mdzad par grags
pa'i rje nga 'dra ma yab sras gsum/
'ol kha mgar phug tu byams pa gling pa'i phyag bzo rje nga
'dra ma khru do ba/
Tol kha rdzing phyi'i 'àu khang. 'og ma'i rten gtso gyang ris
la rje rang gi sku dus su bzhengs pa'i nga 'dra ma phyogs gang nas
mjal kyang der gzigs yod pa lta bu sogs yod ces thos so7
Angag rgyun la bkra shis do kha ma brgyad dang/ nga 'dra ma
bdun zer yang mang po snang ngo/

/RJE RIGS GSUM MA zhes bad sdong gnyis kyi steng sku yod pa Rje Rigs-

/RJE GLING PHUR MA ni par de bzhengs ma thag 'gro ba'i don Rje Gling-
la gnas gzhan du 'phur bas mtshan de ltar gsol ba dang/ 'ga' zhig 'phur-ma
rdo rje gling 'phur ma zhes bzhugs gnas nas rdo rje gling zhes
par 'phur ba yin yang zer/ gang itar par sku'i snyan gyi sne zlum
po zhig yod gsungs/ bdag gis rje gling 'phur ma zhes kha byang

chung mkhyud gang tsam/ phyag gnyis chos 'khor mdzad pa'i pad
sdong gi glegs ral gyi 'og ngos sku chung ngu gnyis yod/ dbu pan
med/ zhabs skyil krung/ gdan gyi mdun du pad ris nyis brtsegs
'dug bya khyung dgon par rje gling 'phur ma'i sku par zhig yod
zer/ mdzo mo mkhar nas le bar drug cu na kha thi kha'i dgon par

yin zer ba dang/ rje gling 'phur ma'i par skong pan chen blo bzang
ye shes kyis phyag nas brgya rtsa song ba'i kha byang can yod ces
thos so/

'dra sku li ma che chung tshon phyed dang brgyad pa gayis 'dug

'dra/ zhabs g.yas rdor dkyil sor bzhag la/ g.yon og tu sor mo

'phan po'i 'JAM DBYANGS zhes kha byang btab yod pa'i 'jam dbyangs 'Phan-po
dmar ser gyi sku dbus gtsang nas gdan drangs pa, zhig dngos su 'Jam-dbyans
mjal bar/ mtha' zlum por yod pa'i leb mo mkhyud gang tsam pa sku
'i g.yas su lanytsas ar pa gsum/ g.yon du tsa ta dhih gsum brtsegs a ra pa
te 'bur (f. 7r) ba mtha skor du bod yi gi ye dha rmā yod pa
zhig 'dug go/
kun mkhyen 'jam dbyangs bzhad pa'i ram thar du/ brtsi bzhag
sbyor lam la slebs pa'i skabs'jam dbyangs bstod sgrub mdzad pa'i
sku de 'od sngon poi gur khyim gyi dbus su bzhugs pa'i 'jam dbyangs
dngos su gyur te zhal gzigs par gsungs pa i sku mgon khang gi 'jigs
byed kyi thugs kar ye shes sems dpa'i tshul du bzhugs shing/ da
ita dgon 'dir 'jam dbyangs dmar ser gyi par sku mtho gang tsam
zhig yod pa 'di thugs dam gyi sku de'i par tsha yin par grags/
'ga' zhig 'di la 'phan po'i 'jam dbyangs zer kyang snga ma'i kha
byang ltar na min nam brtag/
yang rje rin po che'i phyag par gnas po'i 'jam dbyangs zer ba'i
par sku chung ngu gru bzhi "jam dbyangs dmar ser syi sku'i g.yas
g.yon du 'jam dbyangs dam bca'i gzungs yod pa byin can dang/ rje
rin po che i phyag tsha sle'u od dpag med a dam ma zhes sor do
lhag/ pad 'dab nyis rim rgyab yol gyi ri mo can/sku rgyab tu
mthe bong gi rjes dang/ om än hūm/ brtsegs nas yang yod pa mang
po mjal/
KLU 'JIM MA ni mgon po klu sgrub kyis klu yul nas 'jim pa Klu-'jim-
bsnams te phebs pa las bzhengs pa ngo mtshar lha khang gi thub pa ma
KLU 'JIM MĀ dang/ bka' gdams lha khang gi ha shang klu jim ma
Ita bu mang/
/GLANG DAR KHRIMS PHOG MA ni, des bstan pa bsnub ste sku Glang-dar
gzugs bshig pa'i tshe a tsha zhes gsung byon pa dang/ khrag thon Khrims-
pa sogs cho 'phrul bstan pa'i rigs yin zer te sman bla phyag g.yon phog-ma
pa'i mdzub mo bcad pa dang/ sgrol ma'í sku phyag (f. 7v) g.yas
kyi mkhrig ma nas bcad pa dang/ dus 'khor gyi sku zhabs kyi byin
pa nas bcad pa sogs 'ga' zhig angos su mthong/
/DZHAI KŞIM MA ni/ rgyu rin po che sna tshogs 'dus pa las Dzhai-
grub pa ste/ dzhai kşim 'khrul med can dug gi chus byugs na 'od kşim-ma
zer sna lnga 'char bar grags/ sa 'og nas rang byung du thon pa'i
zangs la'ang dzhai kşim yod la/ gser dngul zangs lcags dkar rdo
shel zha nye dkar nag dngul chu dang brgyad po bzhu btul byas pa
bcos ma'i dzhai kşim yin zer ba yang bshad do/
/THUB DBANG RDOR GDAN MA nil gdan gyi steng du rdo rje yod Thub-dbang
pa che chung sna tshogs 'dug pa yul dbus rdo rje gdan gyi li ma Rdor-gdan-
shas che'am snyam/ rgya gar dbus li lha'i bzo rgyun yin pas mdzes ma
shing legs/ rgya gar shar li gnod sbyin gyi bzo rgyun yin pas sku
stod brjid/ rgya gar nub li klu'i bzo rgyun yin pas sku smad phra/
rgya gar shar lis ring bsrel 'khrul med 'dzin pas shar li dang
ring bsrel phan tshun rtogs byed du 'gyur zer,
yang rten byin can gzhan gyis kyang ring bsrel 'dzin pa yod
'dug/ rgya gar dbus li sku sha li ser/ na bza' li dmar las byas
pa'i thub pa la THUB DBANG ZANGS THANG MA zer/ gzhan yang THUB PA
TSHUL KHRIMS MA THUB PA CHOS 'KHOR MA/ THUB PA GSER GLING MA/
THUB PA STA ZUR MA/ THUB DBANG GRONG KHYER MA sogs mang/
spyir sku rgyu gser angul zangs gsum/ tsan dan dkar dmar/
sman 'dam/ ijon dmar/ kā ma rū pa'i rdo/ rdo nag/ li dkar/ li
dmar/ li ser/ li khra/ li smug/ klu 'jim) dzhai kşim sogs (f. 8r)

ming btags so/
/GNAS BCU ME THUB MA dang/ RDOR PHRENG DKYIL THANG ME THUB
MA sogs mes gnod pas ma tshig pa dang/ THOG THUB MA la khro phu Thub-pa
thog thub ma ni khro phu lo tsā ba byams pa'i dpal gyi yab jo Thog-thub-
'phan nam gnubs kyi sngags 'chang nag po ro zan zer ba gshin rje ma
la nus pa thon pa des dgra mang po mthus bsad pas shi nas amyal
bar skyes/ de'i sgrib sbyong du khro phu lo tsā bas yab kyi rus
pa zhugs la sbyangs nas rus chog mdzad de 'jim pa dang bsres nas
sangs rgyas kyi sku mang po bar du btab ste khro phu'i mchod rten
gyi gyad dab tu sbyar nas yod pa las 'khyar ba yin 'dug/ de yang
sangs rgyas kyi sku mdzub gang ma long tsam/ smrI ti'i phyag tsha
che ba dang sku tshugs 'dra ba padma'i rgyab tu wa rtu la'i mu
ne phreng gcig yod pa zhig yin zhes paſ chen d pal ldan ye shes
gsungs/ khro phu lo tsā ba 'di gnubs nam mkha'i snying po'i gdung
brgyud/ phag gru'i slob ma rin po che rgyal tsha dang/ kun ldan
ras pa gnyis kyi dbon po ste/ de gnyis las dge tshul dang bsnyen
rdzogs mdzad/ buddha shri/ mi tra/ kha che pan chen gsum ga bod
du spyan drangs/ byams chen khru brgyad cu yod pa bzhengs/ rigs
sras khro phu sems dpa' chen po bsod nams sengge'o/
/JO NANG THOG THUB MA jo nang 'bum pa chen (f. 8v) po'i nang
du yod zer/ thub dbang mdzub gang ma long tsam dbu'i dpral ba la
dar dpyangs dang snyan gong du me tog beings pa/ mdun du pad gdan
nyis rim/ rgyab kyi gdan la thil btab pa ita bu'i yi ge zhig 'dug
pa dngos su mjal yang yi geci yin mi mthong 'dug/
/PHUR BU LCOG THOG THUB MA ni sku'i dbyibs snga ma dang 'dra
zhing/ de las cung Zad chung/ mdun du padma nyis rim vod/ rgyab.
kyi thil Ita bu de med/ gnyis ka sku rgyu gyo mog ita bu sgra sang
nge 'byung ba yod/
/SNAR THANG THOG THUB MA nið snar thang gi bla ma gtum ston
dang/ gro ston sogs kyis sku de gang gis 'chang yang thog gis mi
tshugs pa yin zer/
yang bla ma zhang/ phag gru/ grub thob thang stong gi sku
mnams la nor bu rnam gsum zhes nang du bzhugs na longs spyod
rgyas zer ba la sgo mang bla ma bstan pa thar pa sogs kyis rje
rin po che'i skus mchog pa med ces tshogs gtam mdzad par grags/ ma chog
yang zhang 'gro ba'i mgon po g.yu brag pa brtson 'grus grags pa'i
sku brnyan SE NA GANG MAr grags pa byin can zhig dang/ phag mo gru
pa rdo rje rgyal po sku'das rjes 'jag spyil du sman dang rin po
che gdul thal bsres pa'i 'dra sku bzhengs pa byin can gsung lan
mang du byon pa la byi bas gdan gyi zur nas sa brus pa akon gnyer
la gsung byon nas slar yang bcos/ sa de mams gzhir byas nas 'dra
sku mang du bzhengs pa la PHAG GRU BRA ZA MA'am/ BYI SA MA zer/
sku bzo ba'i tshe cha shas lhag pa rnams dras pa gzhir byas nas
bzhengs pa'i 'dra sku mnams la phag (f. 9r) gru DRAS SA MA zer/
dras sa ma'i kha byang can gyi sku ga las sa gnon/ g.yon mnyam
gzhag steng nor bu bsnams pa dbu reg/ gong ma mthu bzlog/ zhabs
skyil krung/ mgrin par gnyer ma dang/ 'bol gdan can mtho gang tsam
pa zhig dang/ yang phag gru i sku de las che zhing nyams dod pa/
zhal dbyibs dang sku'i babs snga ma dang 'dra zhing/ chos gos kyi
ri mo 'bur dod can/ g.yon mnyam gzhag steng nor bu med pa zhing
bdag gis mthong la/ rgyal dbang bsod nams rgya mtsho'i rnam thar
du phag gru dras sa ma dang/ byi sa ma rtsod med lnga phyag tu
'byor zhes yod do/
/yang BU STON LCAGS SNYUG MA zhes bu ston rin chen grub kyi
lcags snyug gi dbum bu srog shing gi tshul du bzhugs pa'i 'dra
sku gong ntho gang tsam dngos su mjal zhing/ bu ston NGA 'DRA MA
ni zha lu ri phug gi rten du bzhugs pa'i drung nas kun mkhyen
'jigs med dbang pos gsol 'debs bka' rtsom md zad pa de dus bu ston

du skyes pa dran pa'i tshul mdzad ces rgyal mkhan chen grags pa
rgyal mtshan pa'i zhal nas gsung ba thos so/
/sngon rgyud smad pa mthar rgyas gzhi ka nas ko gru bubs
skabs rgyud smad pa'i slob dpon gyis khyod kyang chu la gshegs
zhes lha mo'i thang ka gtsang por bskur ba gyen du khur nas/ rje
rin po che'i sbyin bdag nang pa lte kha pa'i khyim du rje'i
tshems gcig yod pas gtsang por brub nas khang pa'i 'gram la sleb
kyang chus gnod mi srid/ 'on kyang bltas pas nye 'khor chu g.yas
skor cig na thang ka snyan shal can zhig ong ba mthong nas tog
ra khams chan gyi dpal shul blo bzang ngam/ sde pa mdzo mo ber
ba la lab pas/ khos sha zung zhig (f. 9v) gtad nas longs la khyer
shog dang madang rmi lam legs po zhig byung zer blang nas lha
mo'i bskang 'don pa tshos bsus nas nang du gdan drangs phyi nyin
byang rtse brtan bzhugs 'bul bar gdan drangs pas thang ka mi 'dug
btsal bas byang rtse'i lha mo'i khang du thang ka mying pa zhig
bkram 'dug pa dkon gnyer gyis mthong nas byang rtse'i mkhan po
rdo re gser ri la zhus/ mkhan po phebs par kho mo 'dir sdod ces
gsung lan gnyis byon/ de'i rkyen gyis rgyud smad pa'i lha mo'i
zhal thang da lta byang rtse'i mgon khang du bzhugs/ bal po'i Reference
'khrugs pa'i dus byang rtse'i rdo gcal du mda' zhig dang/ dre'u'i to war o
rjes/ mgon khang mthil du'ang dre'u'i rjes babs zer ba thos so/ Nepal
/SMRI TI'I PHYAG TSHA byang ngam ring/ rta nag gyang mkhar
phyug po/ shangs tshums (or: chums) kyi yul nas 'ong ba thub dbang Smri ti'i
che ba mkhyud gang padma'i rgyab tu rgya gar gyi yi ge phreng gsum phyag tsha
yod pa zhig dang/ bring po thub dang dang/ sgrol ma sor gsum ihag
tsam padma'i rgyab kyi sngags bod yig tu yod pa/ thub dbang chung
ba tshun gang ba/ rgyab tu om al hüm gsum bod yig tu yod pa dang/
yang thub dbang gi sku mkhyud gang las che tsam gcig/ thub dbang
dang sgrol ma mkhyud gang ba mnams yod "dug pas rgya gar nas bsnams Legends
pa'i bar rnams bgres skyon gyis bod du par gsar du bzhengs pa dang/
khams su yang smrI ti'i phyag tsha mang po yod pa 'dra zhes pan
chen dpal idan ye shes kyis gsung/ bka' gdams lha khang du 'ang
smri ti'i phyag tsha thub dbang gi sku par ma sor gsum lhag tsam
gnyis bzhugs/ ngag rgyun la smri (f. 10r) ti'i ma bod kyi khyim
tshang zhig gì thab kha'i nang gi 'bu zhig tu skyes pas khong khyim
der phebs nas g.yog byas/ thab kyi sa blang satstsha dang sku par
btab7 phyugs 'tsho ba'i tshe (?cho) thur ma'i rtse la bcugs nas
bzhag pas zhabs na shing thur gyi shul yod pa de'i rtags yin zer
ba thos/ lo rgyus gzhan du bal po padma rutsi bya ba'i lo tstsha
ba mkhas pa zhig gis pandi ta phra la ring ba dang/ smrI ti gnyis
gdan drangs te phebs pa i lam bar du lo tsā ba sku 'das/ pandi ta
phra la ring ba bod du grong jug mdzad pa rong zom chos bzang
yin par bshad/ kha cig gis smpi ti khams su sku 'das te gtsang
smad rong du sku 'khrungs pa rong zom chos bzang yin zer yang
bka' 'gyur gyi lung gi brgyud yig tu rong zom gyis smri ti la
chos gsan par bshad pas lo rgyus de ma dag pa 'ara'o/
gang ltar smri tis bod skad ma mkhyen par re zhig gtsang rta
nag tu khyim tshang zhig gi ru lug gi rdzi bo byas/ bod du phebs
nas ngu bro ba gsum dang/ rgod bro ba gsum byung/ dang po ni nyin
gcig 'dam rdzab tu khyim de'i bud med kyi bzhon stegs la bzhugs
dgos byung bas/ nged rgya gar du mkhas dgu'i gtsug tu bkur ba las/
da lta bu med kyi stegs su 'dug dgos byung zhes ngu bro/ ra lug
'tsho ba'i tshe khong rnal 'byor pa rten 'brel la mnga' brnyes pa
yin pas rde'u 'ga' ra lug g.yas su song tshe g.yon du bkram/ g.yon
du song tshe g.yas su bkram zhing phyogs gcig tu bsdus pas chog
la/ nang du rde'u nag po re byung na spyang ki 'ong pa'i rtags yin
pas/ de nyid sor mos mnan na spyang ki 'ong mi nus/ mtshan mo
khyim de'i yos 'thag dgos pas (f. 10v) lan gcig gnyid du song ste
mchig gi steng du dbu rgyab pas bud med des/ yos ma pho'am zer/
khong gis nga rang gi mgo de yos gnyis kyi gai che ba yos red gsuns
nas ngu bro/ nyin goig bya khrung srung zhig glag gis bsad nas

A-khu-ching on Art
bya'i ro khong gi pang du lhung bas khyod kyang sa mtha'i bya/ nga
yang sa mtha'i mi gsungs nas ngu bro ba byung/
rgod bro ba gsum ni/ nyin gcig me phung gcig bskyil nas bzhugs
par ri bong gcig kyang khong la mi 'dzem par me la bsros te bsdad
pas dar cig gnyid nas mgo me nang du nyug byas pas gdong gi spu
tshig nas phyogs phyogs su brgyug pas rgod bro/
lan cig mtsho kha zhig tu bzhugs pas mtsho der gnas pa'i klus
khong mkhas pa chen por shes nas bud med cig tu sprul te/ gnyan
gyi rwa co zhig tu 'o ma blug pa sa la bzhag nas phyag 'tshal ba'i
bar la rwa co 'dril te 'o ma thang du bo song bas kho ngo tsha
ste/ phyir bkyed nas sprul pa yang ma bsdus par mtsho nang du lhun
bas rgod bro/
nyin gcig rgya gar na bzhugs dus kyi yon tan mams par skabs
su brjed yod las che snyam du dpyod pa la zhugs pas gcig kyang ma
brjed par thugs la gsal bas rgod bro ba byung/
khong gio khyim de'i phyi sgo'i ma them la ri bong 'dzin pa
rgyu skar phreng ba can/./mtshan mo mkha la rgyud ma mthong nas/
dwangs pa'i mtsho nang 'di na zla ba zhes/ /gzugs bryan zla bar
dzin pa shin tu 'khrul/ /zhes bris yod pa sngon rgya gar du nā
ro pa dang/ smrI ti bla mar brten pa'i lo tsā ba dpyal se tsa bsod
nams rgyal mtshan nam/ 'byung gnas (f. llr) rgyal mtshan bya bas
mthong ste bla ma'i phyag bris su ngo shes nas 'di sus bris dris
par/ nged kyi a bo thang myed kyis bris zer/ da Ita ga na yod
dris pas/ ra rdzi la song zer/ der lo tsā bas mjal khyim der gser
byin nas blus/ rang yul du spyan drangs te 'phrin las rgyas/ bzhugs
par zhus kyang ma gnang bar khams su phebs/ gzhung mang po rang
gyur mdzad/ mtshan brjod 'grel pa sngags don ram gzigs dang/
mngon pa mdzod sogs sde snod du ma'i bshad nyan dang/ phyis bod
skad la byang stel byang chub sems 'grel gyi rnam bshad dang/ smra
sgo mtshon cha sogs brtsams par grags/ d pang lo'i tshogs gsum gsal
bar smra sgo ni bod kyis bris pa'i kha gyar las rgya gar gyi
pandi tas mdzad pa min pa'i shes byed mang du bkod dug/ 'brom
ston pa khams su bla ma se btsun gyi drang na bzhugs dus pandi ta
sgra'i tsher ma can zhes pa dran pa ye shes grags pa las sgra
bslab ces pa'ang pandi ta 'di nyid yin/ phyis khams su 'das pas
yang 'dul gyi lha khang bzhi'i nang tshan idan gyi glang thang
sgrol ma'i nye 'khor dran thang dgon du pangi ta smrI ti'i gdung
'bum mchod rten chen mo na bza'i dum bu tshun chad ia tshul khrims
kyi dri ngad Idang zhing/ gdon bgegs kyi nyer 'tshe las skyob pa'i
byin can bzhugs zhes thos shing/ rgyal dbang bsod nams rgya mtsho
byang phyogs su phebs pa'i lam bar nas smrI ti'i mchod rten mjal
tshul rnam thar du 'dug go/
Ada dung lo rgyus gzhan dag kyang spro bar spobs yod kyi re
zhig de tsam dran thor byas so/
/smras pa/ rgyal ba'i 'phrin las gzugs (f. llv) can du/
shar ba'i sku brnyan byin can 'ga'i/
/ngo mtshar yid kyi me long du/
/bkra ba yi ge'i ris su 'phos/
Zdad 'dun mos gus kyis bakul te/
7mchog gsum sku gsung thugs rten la/
1hag par bya ba byed brtson pa'i/
Zgzur gnas blo Idan de bsngags 'os/
thub pa'i ras bris mthong ba dang
mtshan tsam thos pas don smin pa/
sgra sgrogs skye boli tshogs bzhin du/
7rdul bral chos mig myul thob shog/ /ces rje bdag nyid chen
po sogs kyi sku bryan byên can 'ga' zhig gi lo rgyus cung Zad
brjod pa mnyan par 'os pa'i gtam gyi phreng ba zhes bya ba 'di yang/
btsun gzugs shes rab rgya mtshos chos sde chen po bkra shis 'khyil
gyi rang spyil nas bris pa la ngag sgros ma dag pa'ang yod srid
pas thugs khrel mi mdzad par zhu lags/

Dge-lugs-pa Biography
BIOGRAPHY OF THE THIRD 'JAM-DBYANGS-BZHAD-PA
Skyabs mgon sku 'phreng gsum pa'i dus mchod dang 'brel ba'i mam
thar
ff. 6v-10v from part 12 of vol. 1 (ka) of the Lhasa Zhol New
Printery edition of the Gsung 'bum of A-khu-ching Shes-rab-rgya-
mtsho, 1803-1875.
/de yang ji skad du/ skal bzang bsod nams/ x 'debs/ /zhes
don ldan bsngags pa'i sgra dbyangs rgya mtshos mtha' yas rgyal
ba'i zhing khams rgyas par 'gongs pa bdag cag mnams kyi me tog
phog pa'i lha skal gcig pu kun gzigs ye shes kyi nyi ma skyabs
mgon rdo rje 'chang bka' drin mtshungs med de nyid nges pa'i don
du bgrang yas bskal ba'i snga rol nas yang dag par rdzogs pa'i
sangs rgyas gser thub kyi spyan sngar byang chub mchog tu thugs
bskyed de/ shar phyogs mngon par dga' ba'i zhing khams su rgyal
ba mi 'khrugs pa'i drung du rdzogs smin sbyangs gsum gyis bsdus
pa'i rgyal ba'i sras kyi spyod pa mtha' dag mthar phyin te/ spangs
pa dang rtogs pa'i go phang mthar thug pa mngon du mdzad nas
dag pa dang ma dag pa'i zhing khams rab 'byams su gang la gang
'dul gyi sprul pa i bkod pa bsam gyis mi khyab pas 'gro ba'i don
spyod pa las/ bstan pa 'di la rgyal sras chen po dri med grags pa
nas bzung ste kun mkhyen chen po 'jam dbyangs bzhad pa'i rdo rje
sku phreng gong ma gnyis la thug gi bar du zung 'jug sgyu ma'i
sku la (f. 6) dbang 'byor pa'i skyes mchog dam pa du ma'i
sku'i rnam par rol pas 'phags bod gnyis kar bstan'gro'i don
rlabs po che dpag pa'i yul las 'das pa mdzad cing/ da dung rgyal
ba mams kyi 'phrin las dang lhan cig srid mtha'i bar du sprul
pa'i bkod pa ston par ma zad/ gdan sa chen po 'di nyid du'ang ji
srid khri phrag brgyad kyi grangs 'dzin snam sbyar gyi rgyal
mtshan 'chang ba'i dge 'dun lam sna zin pa sha stag gis gang bar
ma gyur pa de srid du mkhas pa dang grub pa'i skyes rabs kyi phreng
ba zam mi chad pa 'byung bar tshad mar gyur pa'i lung gis grub la/
sku 'phreng 'di nyid kyi mam thar thun mong gdul bya'i snang tshod
tsam gyi dbang du byas na'ang 'dab chags byi'us mkha' lam tshol
ba bzhin du bsam brjod kyi yul las 'das kyang chu thigs tsam zhig
dad pa'i gsos su spel ba la rab byung bcu gsum pa'i bgrang bya
zhe drug pa chu pho byi ba'i lor (1792)/ gangs can mdo smad kyi
yul ljongs dge bcu'i dpal dang ldan pa'i sa yi thig le rtse'i 'dus
ri'i nye 'dabs su grub chen skal ldan rgya mtsho sku 'phreng gsum
pa dge 'dun 'phrin las rab rgyas gang du 'khrungs pa'i rigs rus
cho 'brang phun sum tshogs par gzigs pa mam pa lngas gzigs te ngo
mtshar ba'i bkra shis kyi itas dang bcas sku bltams/
be de dus bla brang gi mgon khyi bor ba dang/ mgon rta zhig ri
la shor ba gnyi ga 'khrungs yul gyi sde 'di'i nye 'khor du song
ba sogs chos skyong phyi bzhin 'brang ba'i rtags mtshan mngon gyur
du bstan/ rje gong ma'i thugs sras nyi zla lta bu mams kyis 'gan
khur bzhes ngos 'jam dbyangs gong ma bdag po chen po nas gser gyi use of the
bum pa'i nang nas brtag bsgril syis thag good (f. 7r) dgos zhes, golden urn
bka' babs pa bzhin rang byung 'phags pa 'jig rten dbang phyug gi
pho brang chen po po ta lar jo bo lo ki shwa ra'i drung du gangs
can mgon po phyag na pad dkar 'chang ba rgyal dbang 'jam dpal rgya
mtsho/ rta tshag rje drung blo bzang bstan pa'i mgon po/ de mo no
mo han blo bzang 'jigs med rgya mtsho/ rwa sgreng no mo han blo
bzang bstan pa rab rgyas sogs bla chen/ bka' blon bzhi sogs mi chen/
lha sa'i am bhan gnyis bcas tshogs te thugs dam zhal 'don rgyun
ring mdzad pa'i mthar am bhan gnyis kyis gser bum dkrug ste mtshan
byang thon pas/ skyabs mgon mthong ba don 1dan de nyid mdo smad
bstan 'gro'i gtsug gi nor bur thob/ de 'dra'i gtam thos'phral gung
thang 'jam pa'i dbyangs nas zhabs brtan skal bzang bsod namsma
bka' rtsom mdzad de me sbrul (1797) zla ba brgyad pa'i tshes gcig
la bsod nams kha dar gyi 'gyed bcas tshogs 'don du tshugs/ rgyal

'Jam-dbyangs-bzhad-pa III
pa'i dbyangs kyis 'khrol ba'i gnas su gyur ba dang/ de'i mthus
sku tshe gcig po 'di nyid la'ang skal ba mchog dang ldan pa'i gdul
bya rin po che lta bu'i gang zag gi don du gnyer bya mthar thug
pa i go 'phang bla na med pa mngon du mdzad pa'i tshul bstan te
de'i zhar la gzhan dag gis ci tsam 'bad kyang bya bar sla ba'i
gnas su ma gyur ba'i legs mdzad spyi dang/ khyad par mdo smad bstan
pa'i rtsa lag chos sde chen po 'di nyid dgon ma lag dang bcas pa'i
chos srid kyi bya ba gang yod grwa ma chag/ gru ma nyams par gong
'phel du mdzad pa sogs sku'i rnam pa de nyid kyis gaul ba'i bya
ba mthar phyin te dpa' bo g.yul las rgyal ba dang/ ded dpon nor
bu lon pa bzhin du dga' spro'i gdengs dang bcas agung lo re bzhi
po shing yos lor (1855) bsam bzhin du ji įtar ngang pa'i rgyal po
gshog yangs bskyod nas mkha' la lding ba bzhin du dag pa'i zhing
khams rab 'byams (f. 10r) su zung 'jug sgyu ma'i gar gyis rtsen
par mdzes pa las/ de ring gi nyi ma 'di de lta bu'i mdzad pa khyad
par can bstan pa'i dus chen yin pas bgres gzhon tshang mas bla
ma'i dus mchod byas pa'i phan yon mdo rgyud dam pas ji ltar gsugs
pa thugs la bzhag stetshogs dang gdung mdun du phebs rgyu/ phyag
mchog bskor bad skyor sbyangs dang zhal 'don sogs klog pa thos
bsam zab rgyas kyi mal 'byor sogs spong ba bsam gtan/ 'dzin grwa
so sos dus bzang/ gshag so so'i steng nas gling me sbar ba sogs
bla ma'i thugs dgongs rdzogs shing rang rang gi tshogs bsags sgrib
sbyangs gnang du smin par eis kyang thugs rje gzigs par zhu/
/zhes skyabs mgon sku 'phreng gsum pa'i dus mchod dang 'brel
ba'i rnam thar 'di ni/ tshogs chen zhal ngo rab 'byams pa dkon
mchog grags pas nan gyis bskul ngor/ btsun gzugs shes rab rgya
mtshos bris palo/

"Jigs-byed
A-khu-ching Shes-rab-rgya-mtsho: 'Jam dpal dus dgra'i dbang po
ma he'i gdong can bcu gsum lha'i khor 10'i rim pa dang po i zab
khrid zin bris jigs mdzad rdo rie'i zhal lung. Part 7 of Volume

ff. lv-
/dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed chen po'i zab lam rin pa dang poli
rnam bzhag cung zad brjod par bya ste/ de yang ston pa yang dag
par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas de nyid kyis dang por thugs bskyed
tshul mdo sngags phal cher "dra/ bar du tshogs bsags nas sangs

og la 'dra min yod pa yig cha rnams su gsal/
1 gang ltar yang rgya gar rdo rje gdan du sangs rgyas pa'i

kyi mchod rten du/ rgyal po zla ba bzang po 'khor sham bha la'i

rgyud/ 'dod chags thabs rgyud sogs gsum las zhe sdang thabs rgyud
kyi gtso bo yin/

da ltar byung ba'i rdzogs sangs rgyas/
/yang dang yang du gsung ba gang/ /zhes rgyud gsungs pa la
'phel 'grib med par bshad pa ltar gleng bzhi dang sbyar na rgyud
rang rang gsungs tshul kyi lo rgyus mi 'dra ba mang po yod pas/

gyis bsdus pas rgyal ba thams cad kyi gsang mdzod 'dzin par bsngags/

mi rung bas/ nub phyogs o rgyan dharmāganydza ste chos kyi gan

btab ste bzhugs par bshad/ ston pas rgyud gsungs tshul gyi lo rgyus

shes kyis/
dur khrod chen po'i dkyil 'khor nas/
/zhes sogs dang/ dbang phyug chen po'i dkyil 'khor las/ /zhes sogs

de nas re zhig rgyud 'di rgya gar du yang mi bzhugs pas/ rnal
'byor gyi dbang phyug grub chen lā 11 ta badzras mtshan brjod kyi/

nas/ orgyan du phebs te rgyud gdan drangs pa la rwa skyo zhang
gsum mthun yang/ ci ltar gsan tshul gyi lo rgyus la zhabs mthil
du sindhu ra sogs rkang mgyogs kyi rdzas byugs te phebs pas mkha'
'gro ma mnams kyis nged cag gi spyi bor byugs pa'i rdzas 'di'i



rkang mthil du byugs pas 'di ltar gyis zhes spyi'i tshugs su
bzhag ces sogs 'dra min mang/ gang itar yang mkha' 'gro ma zhig
chu len du 'ong ba'i rkang pa sa la mi reg par 'gro ba gzigs
nas/ yul 'di na ngo mtshar ba ci yod dris pas/ rdo rje jigs byed
glang mgo can bya ba yod/ de'i gdams pa kho mo dang gzhan dag
gis kyang shes zer bas rjes su "dzin par zhus nas ye shes kyi

'bum pa'i glegs bam gdan drangs pas mkha' 'gro ma rnams kyi
rmi ltas log nas phyir khyer te thur ma zhig gtad nas 'dis ci
(f. 3r) tsam phug pa khyer zhes pa'ang yod/ zhag bdun du blo la
gang zin pa tsam khyer/ de las lhag pa'i gdul bya med gsungs pa
yang yod/ gang ltar yi dam la gsol ba btab ste rtog bdun/ rtog
gsum/ te'u lo pa'i rtog pa/ chu tstshu na dha ra'i rtog pa/ gdong
drug gi rgyud/ dmar nag gi rgyud rnams thugs su chud par mdzad
nas rgya gar du byon pas pan grub mnams kyis ye shes kyi mkha'
'gro ma dang 'dra bar tshad mar mdzad/
gtam rgyud kyi rtog pa ni rwa lugs la rgyud rnam dag tu mi
bzhed kyang/ skyo lugs rgyud du 'dod pa ltar dpal ldan srad
rgyud kyi dam pa mnams kyis khungs su 'dren par mdzad de las a
mo gha badzra ram don yod rdo rje che ba sogs las brgyud pa'i
rim pa mang yang bod du rwa skyo zhang gsum grags che
rwa lo tswa ba rdo rje grags kyis bal po thugs rje chen po
'am menydza gling pa dang/ rgyal po'i chad pas phyag mdzub bead
pas bha ro phyag rdum gnyis las nyi ma gcig la mgo btsugs nas
dbang dang gdams pa rdzogs par gsan/ thugs nyams su bzhes pas
bskyed rim phra rags mthar phyin nas bsam gtan tsam gyis las
bzhi 'grub pa'i skabs la slebs pas mngon spyod mdzad tshul gyi
rnam thar shin tu mang/ sku tshe'i smad la skyid shod stod ne'u
me tog ldan syi gsang sngags chos rdzong du bzhugs shing/ der
sku 'das pa'i gdung ril po ldan mda'i mchod rten gyi bum par
bzhugs/
sne'u rdzong drung chen nam mkha' bzang pos mtshan mo
gtsang por ko gru la 'bras spungs su gdan drangs nas 'jam dbyangs
chos rjer phul bas (f. 3v) sngags khang gi 'jigs byed kyi gzungs
su bzhugs shing/ phyag mdzub gcig de la gnang ba gzungs su bzugs
pa'i'jigs byed kyi shu phyis thridge Thun phun tshogs pa'i
phyag tu byung ba red/ ldan gyi lung pa de'i tshur khar gnyan
io tsā ba dar ma grags bzhugs pas da ita'ang der gnyan mgon byin
rlabs can yod par 'dug/ rwa gnyan gnyis mthu 'gras shor bar
grags kyang gnyan gyis rwa lo 'jigs byed gnam sa gang ba dang/
rwa los mgon po'i Ito ba lung pa ita bu'i nang gnyan lo 'khor

mal 'byor pa nang phan tshun drong tshad myul nas rtogs pa'i
bog 'don pa yin/
kun mkhyen gong mas kyang ldan gyi mdar 'jigs byed gzigs pa
de 'dra'i rten 'brel gyis yin pa 'dra/ gzhan yang sham pos gangs
phab nas grwa pa gcig 'das pa la).
sham po nus mthu che mno'am/
/rwa rgan lo tsā rgas mno 'am/
jigs byed mthu nus chung mno' am/100
rwa mtshon rtse mo zad mno'am/zhes bsdigs pas ma bzod par

/dam nyams gsod pa sngags kyi dam tshig yin/

lta khrid kyi brjed byang snying gi thig le. Part 13 of Volume 2
(Kha) of the Lhasa New Zhol Printery edition of the gsung-'bum.

/de yang rje bdag nyid chen po de nyid kyis bla ma dbu ma pa

pa byung/ de'i tshul rje'i snyan du gsol bas khyed rang bla ma

Rgya ra'i Ita khrid
sngon po'i rgyun sngar ltar byung nas lus gang bas lta ngan bag
chags dang bcas pa sbyangs nas rang bzhin stong pa'i dbyings su
chu la chu bzhag pa ltar slar mi idang ba'i tshul du snyoms par
zhugs pas 'jam dpal zhi khro'i thugs ram pa thams cad mkhyen
pa i ye shes dang ngo bo dbyer med du mos nas snying po nyer lnga
sogs bzla/ slar yang bdud rtsi sngon po'i rgyun sngar ltar byung
nas lus gang bas bdag tu 'dzin pa'i ma rig pas mtshon nyon mongs
bag chags dang bcas pa dag nas rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye
shes dang rang sems ábyer med ro gcig tu zhugs par mos nas rtsa
sngags tshar gsum rjes zlos dang lhag ma mnyam 'don byas te nyer
lnga tsam bzla/ gong du bdag med rtogs pa'i shes rab ral gri'i
mnam par gsal btab/ bdud rtsi'i rgyun gyis bdag 'dzin bag chags
bcas pa sbyangs pa'i dmigs pa rtsal du bton pas spyi dang khyad
par lta ba i sngon 'gror zab/ mjug tu mdun gyi bla ma'i thugs
ka'i ting nge 'dzin sems dpa' ral gri de nyid rmad kyis chad nas
rang gi snying ga'i ral gri la thim (f. 4r) pas shes bya'i gnas
la thogs pa med pa'i shes rab rgyas/ rang sems bla ma'i thugs
bde stong chos sku'i ngang du ro gcig tu gyur ba'i.ngang la rtse
gcig tu mnyam par jog pa sngags kyi thun mong ma yin pa'i lta
khrid du 'gyur ro/
mtshan brjod gang du 'don bla mas ma gsung kyang/ yongs
'dzin ye shes rgyal mtshan gyis 'jigs byed kyi gtor 'bul rdzogs
nas mtshan brjod dang/ dge "dun grub kyi sgrol dkar bstod pa las
byung ba'i las bzhi'i 'phrin bcol sogs tshig kher chod kyis dal
'don byed ces skyil krung gi ri khrod pa zhig las thos shing/
sgrol bstod kyi 'phrin bcol bkra shis ihun por 'jigs byed gtor
"bul gyi mthar sbyor bas gu ge yongs 'dzin gyis kyang gsung ba
yin/ mthar mdun gyi rdo rje 'jigs byed rten brten pa'i dkyil 'khor
rang gi snying ga'i ral gri sa bon dang bcas pa la thim pas rang
gi sgo gsum dang bla ma'i sku gsung thugs dbyer med du mos/ bla
mas gnang skabs de nas gtang rag gi mchod pa dang nyer bsdu sogs
kyang ma mdzad par mandal phul nas grol ba bde mchog gi rgyud
gsungs pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi bkod pa ma bsdus par da lta'ang
bzhugs pa ltar bla ma dang dkyil 'khor gyi snang ba rang sems
dang 'bral med du 'grogs pa'i rten 'brel bsgrigs sam snyam gsungs/
rgyun gyi nyams len du byed na bdag mdun sbrags pa'i tshul
de ltar byas te skyong/ 'di'i yig chung klong rdol bla ma'i gsung
'bum khrod du par yang yod la/ de nyid kyi gsan yig tu lcang
skya rol pa'i rdo rje la gsan pa'i brgyud pa yang dug/
bdag gis khri chen bsod nams (f. 4v) abang rgyal las thob/
de nyid kyis brag rgyab dpon slob blo bzang chos 'phel dang/ des
klong rdol bla ma las gsan pa 'dra gsungs/ 'di nyid nyams len du
byas na rje yab sras kyi rnam thar Itar thun mong ma yin pa'i zhi
lhag zung 'brel myur du skye ba'i rten 'brel gyi gnad dang dgos
pa mang ba'i man ngag khyad par can rgyun shin tu dkon pa mkhan
chen drung yig blo bzang rgya mtsho zhes lung chos kyi mdzod
'dzin pa de nyid kyis kyang sngar ma gsan par bdag gis phul ba
de lta bu yin pas gsan pa tsam lam bzhag par rje bdag nyid chen
po'i rnam par thar pa bzhin man ngag lag ien du thebs pa'i sgo
nas bstan pa dangrang gzhan gyi don rgya chen po grub pa mdzod
ces gdams so/

/bla ma dang ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro la phyag 'tshal lo/
7mkhas grub khyung po'i gdams pa ni gu chos drug la/ nā ro
dang ni gu chos drug gnyis grub mtha' ris med la grags che/
nā ro chos drug la rmi lam bar do'i khongs su bsdus nas grong
jug zur du yod/ nā ros lho brag mar pa la gnang ste dwags polo
bka brgyud la grags che/
ni gu chos drug ni nā ro'i lcam ste sring mo ni gu ma zhes
bya ba rgyal ba rdo rje 'chang las dngos suchos gsan pa des mkhas
grub khyung po la gnang ste shangs pa bka' breyud la grags che
bas shangs chos kyi nang tshan yin/
chos drug ni/ gtum mo lam gyi rmang rdo/ sgyu lus chags sdang
rang grol/ rmi lam gnyid 'khrul rang dag/ bar do rgyal ba longs
sku/ od gsal ma rig mun sel/ 'pho ba ma bsgom sangs rgyas so
/nā ro dang ni gu'i chos drug gnyis ka rdzogs rim yongs
rdzogs re yin zhing/ nā ros mar pa la gnang ba'i chos drug rdo
rje'i tshig rkang/ ni gu mas khyung po la gnang, ba'i chos drug
rdo rje'i tshig rkang zhes gnyis kar rtsa ba re'ang yod/
gnyis ka rdzogs rim mi gsal ba'i bla med kyi iha'i cho ga
gang la'ang sbyar chog/ khyad par rgyud kyi 'byung khung gi
khyad par gyis ma rgyud la 'brel che/ 'di skyabs mgon rdo rje 'chang
gis ra sgreng rgyal ba sngags rams pa blo bzang don grub las gsan
zhing/ de las khri bsod nams dbang rgyal bas sa skya ngag dbang
(f. lv) chos grags kyi yi ge'i steng nas gsan pa go rim khrigs
chags can aka' yang blo nas gang thon tsam byed na/
spyir bskyed rdzogs kyi rigs te lo nā ro sogs rgya gar pan
grub rnams kyis lho brag mar pa sogs la gnang bas dang po rgyud
kyi man ngag 'khrul med kho na yin kyang rjes 'jug dag gis bla
ma'i gsung gi gnad tshul bzhin ma go zhing ma zin pas/ nor 'khrul
shin tu mang po bde gsang 'jigs gsum sogs thams cad la yod pa
las rje bdag nyid chen pos 'khrul pa'i dri ma mtha' dag bsal nas
rgyud dang dgongs 'grel las ci ltar 'byung ba Itar gyi rdo rje
chang gi dgongs pa ma nor ba de sras kyi thu bo mams la gnang
ba'i rgyun da Itar bzhugs pa ltar red/ de bzhin du nā ro chos
drug gi yang khrid yig 'ga' zhig la nor ba shin tu che yang man
ngag gi gzhung dang khrid rgyun snga ma sor bzhag la 'khrul pa'i
dri mas sbags pa rams bsal nas khrid yig yid ches gsum ldan mdzad/
ni guchos drug la rje rang gis yig cha dngos su mdzad pa
med kyang rje rin po che nas brgyud pa'i khrid rgyun gyi gdams pa
Itar rgyal ba dge 'dun rgya mtshos khrid yig rgyas bsdus gnyis
mdzad pa rje'i dgongs pa 'khrul med du gnas/ ngag dbang chos grags
kyi yi ge'i steng nas dmigs pa'i rnam grangs dag gis zur brgyan
te rje'i rang lugs ltar phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs nas nyams su blangs
na legs pa las snga ma'i (f. 2r) khrid yig gi tshig ris tsam byas
na rdzogs rim gyi tha snyad 'thob dka' o
/des na thog mar gtum mo legs par go na dmigs rim deli steng
nas rdzogs rim mthar phyin 'gro bas lam gyi rmang rdo zer ba'i rgyu
mtshan shes dgos/ gzhan phyogs pa'i gtum mo'i dmigs rim la drod
skye ba myur yang rdzogs rim dang 'brel nas nyon mongs spangs tshul
gyi man ngag mi gsal/ zung 'jug gi sku shin tu phra ba'i rlung
sems las sgrub dgos shing/ shin tu phra ba'i sems kyis stong nyid
mngon sum du rtogs pa ma rig pa'i gnyen po dang/ de'i bzhon pa'i
rlung las dag pa'i sgyu ma'i skur bzhengs pas chags sdang rtsa
ba nas spong bas sgyu 'od gnyis ni ma rig mun sel dang/ chags sdang
rang grolzhes pa'i mtshan gyi steng nas go dgos kyang snga ma'i
khrid yig dag las mtshan don mi gsal/



rmi lam gyi mal 'byor gyis gnyid kyi 'khrul pa bsal nas
gnyid chos sku'i bsre ba sogs lam 'bras kyi 'od gsal 'grub pa
dang/ sgyu lus kyi gzhi byed pas de'i yan lag yin/ tshe 'dir lam
gyi rtogs pa mthar thug pa'i sgom ma grub na 'pho ba'i lam gyis
sngags spyod pa'i rten du mtshams sbyar nas sangs rgya nus pas
ma bsgoms sangs rgyas zhes tha snyad sbyar/
sems dben gyi rtogs pa mnyed kyang spyod pa ma grub pas tshe
'dir mchog ma grub na bar dor longs sku 'grub pa'i gdams pa ste
chos drug la dmigs skor re dang/
las dang po pas bag chags jog pa'i thabs su snga ma'i khrid
yig rnams las amigs skor thor bu mang du 'byung/ rdzogs rim gyi
gnad thams cad 'dir tshang dgos pas gtum mo la brten nas rlung
dbu mar (f. 2v) zhugs gnas thim pa'i rtags dang rtags can brgyad
dang bsre ba skor dgr sbyar dgos de byung na 'chi ba 'od gsal
lam gyi 'od gsal du bsgyur nas bar do rgyal ba longs sku grub
kyang chog/ Tshe 'dir Tod gsal ma rig mun sel dang/ sgyu lus chags
sdang rang grol grub kyang chog7 de'i grub pa'i thabs dang yan
lag rmi lam gyi mal 'byor/ tshe 'di dang bar dor ma grub natuke
'chi khar 'pho ba'i rnai 'byor nyams su blangs chog pas lam thun
mong bas rgyud sbyangs/ dbang thob cing dam tshig bsrung/ yi dam
ci rigs pa'i bskyed rim sngon du btang nas/ gzhi dngos po'i gnas
tshul sogs sa bead rdzogs rim spyi dang 'dra?
thog mar bla ma'i rnal 'byor rang gi spyi bo'am ndun gyi
nam mkhar seng ges bteg pa'i rin po che i khri'i steng du ngo bo
rang gi rtsa ba'i bla ma la rnam pa rdo rje 'chang sku mdog akar
po bsgom/ ye shes pa bstim/ skyabs gnas kun 'dus su mos/ sgo
gsum gyis phyag 'tshal/ phyi nang gsang ba de kho na nyid kyis
mchod/ gsol 'debs dang/ ting nge dzin gyi dbang bzhi blang/
mthar bla ma snying dbus su bzhugs pa rdzogs rim spyi 'gro ltar
byas kyang chog/
het de rjes rdor sems bsgom bzlas kyi dod ita bu bka' brgyud.
lugs kyi dag byed a'i stong ra ni/ lus dwangs gsal od kyi rang

na mo gu ru he badzrā ya/ de yang lho brag mar pa lo tsā ba chos

tsha brgyud la rngog kun dga' rdo rjes spre'u zhing gnas gzhi
btab) rngog gdung brgyud bdun pa spre'u zhing rin po che byang
chub dpal ba rje bdag nyid chen po dgung lo nga goig bzhes pa me

rgyal/ gtsang chung chos grags/ spyan snga nyer gnyis pa lha gzigs

ma mang du 'dus/ phyag dpe brtag gnyis kyi gzhung rdo rje mar

brgya dang brgyad cu rtsa gnyis byung/ bar skabs su gdan bzhi'i

Za byed mkha' 'gro'i sbyin sreg
A-khu-ching Shes-rab-rgya-mtsho, 1803-1875: Za byed mkha' 'gro'i
sbyin sreg gi khrid kyi zin bris sdig ltung mun sel. Part 4 (ff.
5) of Volume 3 (Ga) of the Lhasa New Zhol Printery edition of the
gsung-'bum.
Zapal ldan rdo rje mkha' 'gro yi/
zhabs kyi padmor gus btud de/
Zdus mtha'i zhugs dra'i ye shes mes/
7sdig sgrib bsreg pa'i thabs mchog 'god/
de la za byed mkha' 'gro la brten pa'i sbyin sreg gi khungs
ni rdo rie mkha' 'gro'i le'u zhe drug pa las/
slob ma yi ni rkang mthil du/
/gzhu 'dra'i rlung gi dkyil "khor bsam/
Alte bar ye shes me 'bar ba/
Zde yi 'od zer snying gar "bar/
Z'bar bas kun nas 'khrigs par bsgom/
Zpam las byung ba'i mi sdug gzugs/
sdig ni sna yi sgo nas dbyung/
Zde nas khro bo'i gzugs bsgom la/
Zde ni kun nas za bar bsgom/
/om badzra đã ka kha kha khá hi khã hi sarba pã pam đa na na
bhasmi ku ru hüm hüm phat/
ces dang/ slob dpon kun snying gi rdor dbyings dkyil chog rdo rje
byung ba las/
yangs shing dmar po rnams kyi me/
rab sbar rdo rje khro bo yi/
mnyam par bzhag pa snyoms 'jug pa/
til bsreg pas ni sdig bsreg shog/
Zom sarba pā pam da ha na badzra ya swā hā/ zhes dang/
lag pa g.yas pa'i mthil du til nag po las sdig pa'i gzugs
brnyan byas la/ hum d bus su bsam pa'i mdzub mo dang mthe
bos sbyin sreg bya'o/ de nas sbyin sreg gi thab khung las
byung ba'i 'bar ba'i phreng ba kun tu 'khrugs pa'i rdo rje'i
mes de'i lus la babs pas sdig pa rnams bsreg par bsam par
bya'o
zhes gsungs/
kun mkhyen (f. lv) 'jam dbyangs bzhad pa'i dbang gi bried byang
las lung 'di drangs nas/
'di ni kho bo'i bla ma rgyud chen rdo rje 'chang gi phyag len
la til dang mar la sdig pa'i gzugs byas nas sdig sgrib gdon
bgegs thams cad bkug nas za byed rdo rje mkha' 'gro sogs la
brten nas sbyin sreg byed tshul gyi khrid thob pa de'i man
ngag gi gzhung bla na med par snang ngo/
/zhes gsungs pa 'di mnams shes byed kyi khungs rnam dag yin pas
thog mar bkod pa yin la/ 'di'i khrid rgyun ni rje bdag nyid chen
po las mkhas grub thams cad mkhyen pa sogs dpal ldan srad rgyud
kyi dam pa mnams la brgyud de/ srad rgyud dkon mchog yar 'phel las
kun mkhyen 'jam dbyangs bzhad pa'i rdo rjes gsan tshul rnam thar
sogs su gsal/
de nas khi chen Age 'dun phun tshogs/ khri ngag abang mehog
ldan/ rgyal dbang bskal bzang rgya mtsho/ pan chen dpal ldan ye
shes/ yongs "dzin ye shes rgyal mtshan/ tshe gling slob doon iha
rtse ye shes bstan'dzin/ 'bras blo gling rgyal rong dge bshes rje
tshul khrims nyi ma'i zhal snga nas las bdag dge slong shes rab
rgya mtshou yig chung nyer gcig las byung ba'i cho ga'i steng nas
thob pa yin pas gzhung ni delo/
7gsung bshad la/ 'di la 'byor na yongs grags kyi zhi thab che
ba khru gang ba de nyid cha gsum du (f. 2r) byas pa'i cha gnyis zhi
thab 'bring po/ de nyid cha gsum du byas pa'i cha gcig la zhi thab
chung ngu'i tha snyad yod pas khru gang la cha gsum byas pas thab
sor brgyad/ de'i khar yongs grags kyi mu ran kha khyer sor bzhi pa



Za byed mkha' 'gro: A khu ching
cha gsum du byas pa'i cha re re/ de'i phyir stegs bu sor do cha
gsum du byas pa'i cha gcig gis gri bzhi byas/ thab kyi nang cha
gsum du byas pa'i dbus su lte ba/ de'i phyir padma 'dab brgyad/
Ite bar gri gug gam rdo rje rtse inga pa gyen 'greng/ kha khyer
la rdor phreng] zur bzhir zla phyed rdo rje gyen 'greng/ phyogs
bzhir bu ga gru gsum bzhi byas pas dbyibs
'di Ita bu 'ong/
dbus gtsang na 'di 'dra lcags dang zangs las bzos pa las
sku 'dra khyab che ba mi 'ong/ sku yod na mu ran khar 'jog/
thig 'debs pa'i srol med pa dra/
gzhung du/ me rdog po du ba med pa snod du bzhag gsungs pas
sku dang thab nges can du mi dgos/ gyo mo'am g.yam pa ita bu'i
steng me du ba med pa bzhag nas phul bas chog/shing sogs du ba
can mi byed/ skyabs sems sngon du btang/
khyad par sems can thams cad kyi don du myur ba myur bar
rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi go phang thob par bya/ de'i phyir
rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i sbyin sreg la 'jug snyam pa gsum sogs bya/
'dir dus pa'i man ngag tu byas nas bgegs mthar_byed dang/ 'jigs.
byed lta bu'i nga rgyal la gnas nal khangga dhri (or: khadga dhrl)
ka sa ma hrih striḥ sa bsangs pa/ gzhung du rang gi sngags kyis
bsangs zhes pa'i don yin/
spyi 'gro ltar a mrī tas bsangs kyang chog/
de'i tshe rang yi dam gyi lhar gsal ba'i snying ga'i (f. 2v)
sa bon las khro bo'i tshogs 'phros nas thab dang/ me dang/ rdzas
sogs la gnas pa'i bgegs bsangs/ dpung bzang itar mchod rdzas sogs
la log 'dren zhugs nas nyon mongs skye ba sogs sems rgyud las su
mi rung bar byed pas de la bsrung ba byas pa yin/
pan chen dpal idan ye shes kyi dris lan zhig tu/
thog mtha' bar gsum du rang tha mal par gnas pa dang/ yi
dam gyi lhar bsgom pa la khyad med gsung ba zhig yod kyang/
lha'i rnal 'byor la gnas pa'i thun mtshams yin na des chog
la/ gzhan du lhar bskyed pa bde/ de nas thab dang sku yod med
gang ltar yang shū n.ya tā'i sngags don legs par dran nas tha mal
gyi snang zhen stong par sbyangs pa mnyam gzhag nam mkha' lta bu'i
stong nyid dang/ de'i rjes thob sgyu ma lta bu'i stong pa'i
ngang las thab yod na hūm dkar po las rdzogs par bskyed la/ de'i
dbus su ye shes kyi me dmar po gru gsum pa dang/ med na stong pa'i
ngang las ye shes kyi me amar po gru gsum pa zur gcig rang dang/
gnyis g.yas g.yon du bstan pa/ de'i dbus su sna tshogs pad nyi'i
gdan la hüm mthing nag las za byed rdo rje mkha' 'gro dam tshig
pa bskyed/ ye shes pa bcug/ dbang bskur/ rgyas gdab ste bod snga
ma dag gis yan lag bzhi rdzogs zhes tha snyad sbyor/
sa bon/ phyag mtshan/ sku rdzogs pa las bskyed pa la cho ga
gsum bskyed zer/
dir hūm mazad kyi phyag rgyas rdo dril 'dzin par gsungs pas
lag pa gnyis rdo rje khu tshur byas/ g.yas pa steng du bzhag la
rgyab sbyar/ mthe chung màud/ (f. 3r) mdzub mo anyis cung Zad bkug
pa 'dod rgyal dang/ mdzub mo gnyis bsgreng ba ni hūm mdzad kyi
phyag rgyalo/
/sku gzugs 'ga' zhig la phyag gnyis 'khyud rgya mdzad pa
dang/ zhabs g.yas brkyang ma yin par tsog pur bzhugs pa lta bu
byas 'dug/
pan chen gong ma'i gsung du cho ga gsum bskyed dang/ zhal
gnam du gdangs shing mche ba bzhi gtsigs pa/ thod skam Inga'i dbu
rgyan dang/ rlon pa lnga bcu'i do shal 'phyang ba/ stag sham can/
khro nyams yongs su rdzogs pa/ zhabs gnyis sdig sgrib 'joms pa la
