Za byed mkha' 'gro: A khu ching
dpa' ba'i nyams kyis zlum por bzhugs pa/ zhes gsungs/
thugs ka'i hüm gi 'od zer gyis bsgoms pa dang 'dra ba'i ye
shes pa spyan drangs pa mdun gyi nam mkha' am/ me tshang gi shar
lhor bzhugs pa la rang gi thugs ka nas spros pa'i lha mo mchod
rdzas thogs pa rnams kyis mchod de snying gar bsdu/
dzah zhes pa'i skabs shel bum du 'bru blug pa itar dam ye'i
sku (or: sgyu, spu?) lus thams cad nyis brtsegs/
hüm zhes pa'i skabs dam tshig pa'i sku'i cha de dang der ye
shes pa'i cha de dang de zhugs/
bam zhes pa'i skabs 'o chu ltar dbyer med du 'dres/
hoh zhes pa'i skabs ji srid sdig sgrib sbyangs pa'i 'phrin
las ma rdzogs kyi bar thugs sems drang pos mnyes bzhin bzhugs par
bsam dgos par yongs "dzin rin po che'i phyag bzhes ltar bdag gi
bla mas yi ge bzhi'i bar thag bsring nas brjod pa yin pas spyi
'gro'i mig Itos tsam ma yin par rang rang gis lag tu lon (?) pa
byed gsungs/
panytsa kū la rigs lnga zhes pa yin pas rgyal ba sras bcas
dbang lha rigs lnga bum pa thogs pa'i rnam par spyan drangs te
mchod/ (f. 3v)
rang gis mdun gyi lha la dbang bskur bar gsol ba btab pas
dbang lha'i zhal nas sngags brjod de chu rub kyis dbang bskur
lus gang/ dri ma dag/ chu'i lhag ma spyi bor 'khyil ba las rigs
bdag mi bskyod pas dbu brgyan par bsam/
bsdu na ye shes pa dang dbang lha mnyam du spyan drangs kyang
chog/
byin gyis brlabs pa'i mchod pa dang nang mchod yod na de dang
med na rdo rje thal mo sbyar la yid kyis phul/ mi bskyod rdo rje
ye shes che nas/ rdo rje mkha 'gro la phyag tshal zhes pas
bstod/
til nag po 'bul thub pa'i tshod la sdig pa'i gzugs bzo
am/ gang itar me long ngam snod du bzhag/ 'ga' zhig lhag ma phyir
len pa mi legs pas sdig pa lhag med du 'dag pa'i rten 'brel du
gang bshams pa thams cad 'bul/
'bru lhag na mnyam du lhag pa lha la ma gus par 'gyur ba dang/
de 'dra la sa bon 'joms pa'i ltung byed kyi dus dran kyang e chags
shes aka'/ mar dang til bsres nas sdig pa'i gzugs bzo'am/ me long
steng du til kho nas bzo'ang yod/ de nyid sna sgor bzung la/ rdo
rje mkha' 'gro dang/ pan chen chos rgyan gyi gsung ltar rang gi
rkang mthil du rlung dkyil gsal 'debs pa'am yig chung ltar gsang
gnas su yam las rlung dkyil sngon po gzhu'i dbyibs can/ lte bar
ram las me'i dkyil 'khor dmar po gra gsum pa/ snying gar mi shigs
pa'i thig le rlung dang bcas pa'i steng tsam du sdig sgrib kyi
ngo bo pam nag po/ de las 'od zer nag po lcags kyu Ita bu lus kyi
stod smad bar gsum gyi rtsa sbubs thams cad khyab par 'phros/ thog
(f. 4r) med nas bsags pa'i sdig sgrib dam tshig nyamsan Chag
sogs mchog dang thun mong gi dngos grub bsgrub pa la bar du good
pa'i nyes ltung ji snyed yod pa dang nad gdon bar chad thams cad
od zer nag po'i mam par bsdus nas pam la thim/ gsang gnas kyi
rlung gis ite ba'i me gdung bas sdig sgrib gdon bgegs thams cad
'dus pa'i pam de nag na ra ra mgrin pa nas brgyud de sna'i rtser
slebs pa na sdig pa rwa can gyi mam par gyur pa rlung phyir rgyu
ba dang mnyam du thon nas til mams la thim par bsam ste 'bul ba
'am/ thim pas til re re'ang ngo bo thog med nas bsags pa'i sdig
ltung dang/ rnam pa sdig pa rwa can mi sdug pa'i rnam par bsam ste
zhal du phul bas thugs rgyud zag med kyi bde ba dam pas tshim par
bsam/amtheb mdzub sam (sic!)/ mtheb srin sbyar ba dgang gzar
blug tu mos kyang rung la til blangs te rlung phyir bus la nad du
bskor nas phul/ ro malog sgo nas mar thon pa mes bsreg pas thal
ba'i ming tsam yang med pa bzos song snyam du sngags dang bdag



Za byed mkha' 'gro: A khu ching
gis tshe rabs 'khor ba thog med nas bsags pa'i sdig sgrib dam
tshig nyams chag thams cad shi ntam (read: shāntim) ku ru ye swā
hā/ zhes pa'i spel tshig dang bcas brjod/
sems can thams cad kyi sdig sgrib kyang snying ga'i pam
la bsdu ba'am/ phyir thon pa'i gzugs la bsdus nas phul bas de dag
gi sdig sgrib sbyangs nas rdzogs byang la bkod par bsam/
sngags don/ om gyi a u ma gsum gyis rdo rje gsum mtshon tshul
dran nas brjod pas rtse mo itar phan yon bdun 'thob/
badzra dā ka rdo rje mkha' gro/
kha kha gsol gsol lam zo zo/
khā hi khā hi gsol zhig gam zo zhig gam (f. 4v) za ru chug
gnyis/
sarba pā pam sdig pa dang sdig pa'i bsam pa can thams cad/
da ha na sreg/
bhasmi ku ru thal bar mdzod/
hüm hüm bde stong d byer med kyi sa bon/
phat phat ngan song gsum du 'phen pa'i sgrib pa khos shig/
swā hā gzhi tshugs zhes pa'am legs pa sbyin/ /zhes pa'o/
kun rig fik chen las/
hum ni gsal byed ha dang ma/
/dbyangs kyi ū gsum tshogs pa las byung bas om dang hüm
gi thig le ngar 'bod pa sngags btu gang las kyang mi 'byung
bas ma dag pa'o/
gsungs la/ don ni nges tshig gis tshul gyis ū phyis nas ha na ti
Tjoms byed la 'jug pas thugs rje chen po'i thabs kyis sdug bsngal
dang ma rungs pa thams cad gzhom pa ste/ rtse mor/
yi ge hūm ni ci yin brjod/
\/sdug bsngal 'chos shing 'joms par byed/
srid pa'i zhags pa good byed cing/
Zgdug pa spangs shing gsod byed pa'i/
hüm ni mchog tu dran par bya) /zhes so/
7pan chen gsung du hüm hūm phat phat ces pa med/ mthar mchod
bstod dang yig brgya brjod/ ye shes pa rang bzhin gyi gnas su
gshegs/ dam tshig pa thab dang bcas pa me 'bar ba'i rnam par bsam
la rdo rje me'i phyag rgya bya/ me ma (or: ya) shi bar 'jog pa'i
long med na 'o ma sogs kyis gzhi la/ ntshams lta buli skabs phyi
rol tu mi 'dor bar nang du bsags nas 'jog
skabs gzhan du chu la bskur ba dang/ rlung la 'phyar ba dang
sa gtsang sar skyel ba gang bde bya/ phyag khrid byed na bla ma
rang gis sbyin sreg tshar gcig gtong ba'i srol yod, 'di'i zhal shes
kyi rigs sngon chad yi ger 'khod pa mi snang zhes (f. 5r) pan chen
dpal ldan ye shes gsungs/
'di nyid sdig ltung spyi dang dam tshig nyams chag sbyong ba
la rgyud dang grub chen du ma dang/ rje'i gsung du yang bsngags
brjod che zhing/ rje yab sras sogs dpal ldan srad rgyud dang dben
sa snyan brgyud kyi dam pa gong ma mnams kyis thugs dam du mdzad/
khyad par smin grol ngag dbang 'phrin las lhun grub pa khong
grwa rkyang gi dus pan chen blo bzang chos rgyan la skye brtag
zhus par/ bde ba can du skye gsungs/ phyis dge 'dun gyi akor la
'dzem bag dang bcas har gdong khams tshan dge rgan du bzhugs/ de'i
rjes slar yang paņ chen de nyid la ming 'di zer ba'i grwa pa phyi
mar gar skye zhes yi ge phul bar/ dmyal bar
skye zhes lan
gnang/ de'i sdig sbyong du za byed mkha' 'gro'i sbyin sreg tshar
mang po sgrub nas yang zhus pas bde ba can du skye bar lung bstan
pa dang/ sbyong rgyud las/

/dmyal ba chen por skye ba yi/

Za byed mkha' 'gro: A khu ching
/gdon mi za bar bde 'gror skye/ /zhes za byed mkha' 'gro'i
sbyin sreg gi sgo nas sdig pa sbyang ba'i phan yon gsungs pa ltar
'di 'dra ba'i sdig sbyong gnad du 'gro ba re la brten pa gal che
J'air 'bad dge ba'i gzi brjid kyis/
sdig ltung mun pa'i dpung bcom ste/
Zbla med snang ba dam pa'i gter
/lus can padmo'i dpal gyur cig/
ces za byed rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i sbyin sreg gi khrid kyi zin
bris sdig ltung nun sel ces bya ba 'di yang rje btsun bla ma dam
pa yang dag pa'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen tshui khrims nyi ma'i zhal
snga nas las 'di'i zab khrid mnos pa'i skabs/ btsun gzugs shes
rab rgya mtshos rang a gi dran gsor bkod pa'o/

logy, Gangtok, 1967.



Klu'i bum gter
A-khu-ching Shes-rab-rgya-mtsho, 1803-1875: Klu'i bum gter go
gdams pa'i gsal byed rin chen bum bzang. Part 24 of Vol. 3 (Ga)
of the Lhasa Zhol New Printery edition of the gsung-'bum.
Ina mo gu ru nā gendra rā dzā, ya/
Z'dir kun mkhyen 'jam dbyangs bzhad pa'i klu'i bum gter gyi
steng nas khrid lan gsum mnos pa'i skabs kyi brjed tho ni/
phyogs bcu'i rgyal ba mnams kyi thugs la dgongs rgyu gzhan don
kho na las med/ sems can thams cad drin can gyi mar gyur pa
sha stag yin pas bde ba thams cad la 'god dgos/
god
rgyu'i bde ba dang de sgrub pa'i thabs grangs med7 de'i nang
nas 'jig rten gyi khams kyi mi'i tshe bsod chos 'byor bde skyid
'phel ba'i thabs bsten na de la brten nas rang gis chos sgrub.
ste sangs rgyas kyi go 'phang btsal dgos/ 'jig rten gyi bde
skyid de yang/lazam buli gling 'dir chu klung ji snyed cig
'bab cing/ nas/ de ni klu yi bdag po de yi mthu apal yin/ 7zhes
yul de'i klu dga' ba dang dar ba dang 'phel ba gal che/
de'i stobs kyis klu'i rgyal po rgya mtshos zhus pa dang/
ma dros pas zhus pa'i mdo sogs las sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
klu'i yul du spyan drangs tshul gyi mnam thar la dpyad rgyu
dang go rgyu mang/ des na klu'i bum gter byed par "dod na
rgyal dbang lnga pa chen po'i gzungs gzhug 'khrul spong du
khungs med kyi rang bzo bkag pa itar mdo rgyud kyi dgongs pa
ma nor ba gal che/

rje 'chang dkon mchog yar phel las 'di'i khrid gsan te gsung
bshad gzhir bzhag pa'i cho ga mdzad pa'i steng nas khrid rgyun
yod/ spyir bum gter la rigs mang ba thu'u bkwan rin po che'i
gsung du/ rigs Inga/ sa'i lha mo/ klu/ rdzas kyi gter rnams
gsungs pa lta bus mtshon nas shes/

bzhi yod/ 'jam dbyangs bzhad pa'i rdo rje dang/ khri ngag dbang
mchog ldan gyis mdzad pa'i bum gter sogs phyag len cung zad
'dra min mang/ las so so'i bum gter la/ zhi bar rdzas spyi

jam zhing i klu la mi gnod pa/ nad dmigs bsal de dang de

dang/ rgyas par tshe bsod chos 'byor rgyas pa'i rdzas dang/ de
lta bu'i spel tshig dang 'dod gsol/ sa bkra bzang bar sba ba
dang/ dbang la 'di zos pas khams gsum abang du 'gyur ro zer ba
Ita bu'i rdzas dang/ de mthun gyi spel tshig sbyor zhing/ abang
gi rten 'brel la bsngags pa'i sar sba dgos/ gtsug lag khang gi
rmang gzhi'i bum pa ni de'i mthil du 'jog/
a mchog gi grub brnyes kyi gsung las (f. 2r) zhes pa darpā.
na ā tsar.ya'am pandi ta 'gro ba'i me long zhes tshe'i rig
'dzin brnyes te tshems lan nyi shu brjes pa'i grub chen des
mdzad pa'i kri ya sam mutstsha'i lung drangs pa yin/
gnas ri rtse/ ri sked/ ri zhol/ nags tshal sogs su 'bul
tshul mi 'dra ba yod/ sa abyibs kyi' bkod pa dang/ chu'i kha
dog dri ro las der gnas pa'i klu mi 'dra tshul kri ya'i lung
sho lo ka dang pos mdor bstan nas/ lhag mas zhing dang chu mig
la klu mtha' yas gnas pa sogs so so'i gnas ma 'dres par shes
na klu de dang de gtso bor byas pa'i bum gter byas na shin tu
legs/ de 'dra ma shes na 'dir gsungs pa ltar spyi 'gro'i cho
ga sbyar bas 'thus/ rin po che i bum pa rkun po sogs kyis khyer
nas gter mi brtan pa'i dogs pa yod pas sa gter dang chu gter
la mi legs gsungs/
des na rdza sogs kyis rung/ bum pa'i kha dog spyir btang
dkar po dang/ zhi rgyas dbang drag la dkar ser dmar nag bya/

Klu'i bum gter: A-khu-ching
mdzod bum ni khyim gter khang pa'i nang du sba/ che chung gi
tshad rgyud ltar che 'bring 'dus pa dang dus 'khor gyis rnam
rgyal bum pa'i tshad sngags rim las gsungs pa ltar dang/ ma
mtha' yul de'i bre gang shong ba gal che/ da ita nor rdzas la
sred pas gter sgrub mkhan mang yang nang du rdzas phor gang
las mi shong ba rten 'brel mi legs/ bum pa gcig las med na
mdun rgyab mi nor ba'i phyir mdun du rin po che cha dgu pa
las gzhan ri mo sna tshogs dgos pa'i nges pa med/ klu abang
gtso 'khor lnga'i bum pa so sor yod na mdun du rang rang gi
phyag mtshan dang/ (f. 2v) bum pa gcig la phyogs so sor bris
chog/ 'byor pa rgyas pa dang/ sa dpyad ngan pa bsal ba sogs
la sku med par gter rdzas kyis bkang nas nam mkha' mdzod kyi
rang bzhin du byin gyis brlabs pa gnas legs nyes la ltos pa
med par gang 'dod sar bzhag chog pa mchod pa gar yang phul
chog pa dang 'dra/ lha bum la klu dbang byed na de'i sku dang/
klu bum la klu so so'i sku dgos/ mdzod bum dang klu bum yod
kyang chog/
rdzas la rag gam ra gan zha nye sogs mi rung bas de dag
gi dong tshe yang bzhag mi chog/ bra bo ni yongs grags gros
zhes 'bras bu nag po zur gsum pa dang/ shangs tshe ni kha
cig gis rta sho'i 'bras bu zer yang ske tshe dang dbyibs 'dra
ba'i rtsa 'bras bu can ri 'gor yang yod/, yongs grags kyi sran
ma ni gter rdzas su rung bar gsungs pas/ 'ga' zhig gis sran ma
mi rung zer ba sman gyi srad ma la ngos 'dzin zer mkhan yod
khyung sder dang gla rtsi sogs klu la gnod pa'i sman gyi dris
kyang ma -gos pa dang/ sha chang gis ma sbags pa shin tu gal
che/ ye shes kyi bum pa'i nang du klu sman gyi rigs nges par
mi dgos kyang/ klu bum la klu gtor ltar gyi klu sman cha tshang
gal che/ bum pa dgr yod na re re la rang rang gi sku sngags
spel dang bcas pa re re 'jog/ bum pa lnga yod na shar dang
shar lho'i klu la bum pa gcig sogs de'i rigs 'gre/ gnyis las
med na de bzhin gshegs par bum pa gcig dang/ klu brgyad gtso
bo dang bcas par gcig bya/ bum pa gcig gi smad la klu dang/
(f. 3r) stod cha la de bzhin gshegs pa gtso 'khor 'jog/
khri ngag dbang mchog ldan dang 'jam dbyangs bde ba'i rdo
rje'i gsung ltar na sku rnams ma bsgril bar leb mor dbus su
gtso bo/ phyogs mtshams su 'khor mnams zhal gtso bo la phyogs
pa'am/ thams cad gtso bo dang lta phyogs mthun par 'god pa dang/
sku dang sngags spel g.yon nas bsgril te bkod kyang rung bas
gang bde bya/ 'on kyang srad rgyud pa'i phyag bzhes la lha
klu'i bum pa gnyis sam/ gcig las med tshe shog bu gcig la thog
mar klu dbang rgyal po/ de nas mdun gyi byang sems/ de nas g.yas
kyi byang sems/ de nas rgyab kyi byang sems/ de nas g.yon gyi
byang sems rnams mthar chags su bris/ steng du gdugs dang/
'og tu mtsho/ mthar mchod rdzas mams bris kyang chog/
de nas g.yas phyogs nas nang du bsgril bas gtso bo dbus
dang/ 'khor bzhi go rim bzhin phyogs bzhir 'bab pa ltar yongs/
yang shog bu gcig la klu dbang gi sngags rang gis gang 'dod pa'i
spel tshig dang bcas 'go nas bsgril ba sku'i mdun gyi thugs ka'i
thad du 'bab pa byas nas 'jog/
de bzhin du shog bu goig la klu gang gtso bor byed pa thog
mar bris/ der mthud nas shar dang shar lho'i klu sogs rim par
bris/ de'i "dab la gdugs/ rgyal mtshan/ ba dan sogs mchod rdzas
kyi bye brag sna tshogs dang/ steng du gdugs dang bla re/ log
tu mtsho dang chu ris bris/
g.yas nas nang du bsgril na gtso bo dbus su 'ong zhing
'khor lhag mas bskor ba Ita bu dang/ gdugs dang (f. 3v) ba dan
chu ris kyis kyang steng og phyogs mtshams kyi mtha' bskor ba
'byung/ gzungs gzhug gi dod du klu mnams kyi sngags spel tshig
dang bcas pa go rim sngar ltar mthar chags phreng gcig tu bris



Klu'i bum gter: A-khu-ching
la 'go nas nang du bsgril te sku gzugs kyi thugs ka'i thad kyi
mdun du btsugs nas 'jog pa srad rgyud rdo rje 'chang gi gsung
rgyun 'khrul med yin/
de dag la na bza' dang skud pa sogs gang bde bya/ spyir
rgyal dbang gi 'khrul spong ltar gzungs gzhug 'go nas drii ba

shin tu legs/ klu'i bum gter la phyag len 'di ltar na sngags

sku dang/ mdun du sngags spel btsugs/ gter rdzas kyis bkang/

len yin, bum pa dgu yod na padma 'dab brgyad kyi lte 'dab dang/

Klu'i bum gter: A-khu-ching
byed yin nam snyam/ ri mo gsum pa ni dung dkar g.yas 'khyil la
byed/ zhi sogs las mthun gyi phyag mtshan bsgyur kyang chog/
gyon phyogs nas rig mas bsten pa gnod sbyin 'khor lo'i sgrub
chog sogs la yod/ klu'i abang phyug gi sgrub thabs ni mgon po
klu sgrub kyi yin pas gong gi slob dpon zhes pa de yin/ zan
ril la sor rtses rjes gtod pa'i (f. 5r) zan gyi kham phor brgyad
du 'o ma dang klu sman btab pa ni kri ya nas bshad pa'i gtor
ma yin/ zhag bdun la sogs par sgrubs nas sa la sba na rgyas par
ito 'phye'i thig dang/ min kyang sa'i bdag po sogs la bsang
dang akar gtor btang/
sa brtag bslang sbyangs bzung rgyas bsdus skabs bstun bya/
'dom gang tsam brus la nang du rdo khang brtsigs/ de la zhal
ba dang klu sman btab/ rlan gyis mi gnod ched steng og kun
tu shug pa mang du blug/ de'i nang du pad gdan la bum pa gnyis
yod na brtsegs nas bzhag/ zangs gzhong gtsang mar ra dkar mo
dang ba akar mo'i 'o ma sha chang gla rtsi dang dri ngan pas
ma sbags par thad ka der bzhos nas ma god par blug na klu
sman gtsang ma yin gsungs/ par mnying du spos akar po dang/
par gsar du pog dkar po zhes pa brda gsar rnying gi khyad par
las don gcig par dbus pa blo gsal sogs kyis bshad de/ spos
snod la pog phor zer ba ita bu'o/
lag pa gnyis thal mo byas pa'i sor mo rnams kyi rting
pa sbyar/ lag mthil phye/ gung mo gnyis lto sbyar la rtse phye/
sor mo thag ma mams kyi rtse cung Zad phyir bkyed pa ni rgyud
las gsungs pa'i klu dga' bar byed pa'i phyag rgya 'khrul med
yin par sgeg pa'i rdo rje'i rgya gzhung las 'byung bar kun
mkhyen gong mas gsungs/
| g-yon khu tshur bras pa'i mthe bong dang mthe chung
brkyangs pa'i mthe bong gi steng g.yas pa'i sor mo rnams bsgrengs
pa ni gdeng ka sbrul mjug dang bcas pa'i phyag rgya yin pas klu
dga' bar byed pa'i phyag rgya la de itar byed pa nor ba yin/
rgyas par (f. 5v) byed na nyin thun dang mtshan thun byas te
sngags rgyun ma chad pa bya/ klu sgrub kyi sgrub thabs su shar
ngos su sba gsungs pa longs spyod phel ched yin na dgon gnas
'di lta bu'i mdun ri'i ngos nas zhal tshur bstan nas kha sprod
du sba zhes gsung bshad gsal bar gnang/
deng sang gi lag len 'di dang mi mthun pa ltar yod sa
gzhan du chu 'go nas yar gom pa dgu song ba'i tshod tsam du klu
gter kha chu mig la bstan nas sbas te klu tho bslang 'dug pa mi
rung ba ang cher med/ 'on kyang chu mig gi 'go nas mar gom pa
dgu song ba'i mtshams nas kha yar chu 'go la bstan nas bum pa
gnyis chu mig dang kha sprod du bzhag na der gnas pa'i klu dar/
de la brten nas sbyin bdag dar ba yin/ khang pa la yang de ltar
sba ba klu sgrub kyi sgrub thabs kyi àgongs pa srad rgyud pa'i
gsung rgyun ma nor ba yin/
las so so'i sngags spel gyi gnad las dmigs bsal de dang
de'i rdzas dang spel tshig amigs pa sogs sngar ltar yin la
dpa' ris dam chos kyis brag dkar dka' bou rin po cher drag po'i
klu gter ci 'dra yin zhus par/ sku rtsed kyi rnam pas/ rnal
'byor pa red mod/ bum pa nag po/ nang du ngan rdzas/ drag po'i
spel tshig de mthun gyi dmigs pa sogs phal cher klu gtad lta
bu yin pas drag po'i gter gyi dgos pa med gsungs/
bkra shis sgo mang gi chos grwa gong ma rgya bskyed pa'i
skabs su bka' rtsom mdzad tshul sngon gyi dpe rnying bris ma
zhig gi mjug na 'dug/
de dus kun mkhyen gong ma sgo (f. br) mang bla ma yin pas
de dang/ slar dgon gsar 'debs gnyi ga'i ched du gnang bar nges/
'di'i khrid rje rin po che nas dpal ldan srad rgyud kyi dam pa
rnams la rim par brgyud de kun mkhyen 'jam dbyangs bzhad pa/



Klu'i bum gter
khri chen ngag dbang bkra shis/ gser kha pa ngag dbang bsod
nams rgya mtsho/ brag dkar dka' bcu rin po che/ de las gsan pa
yin gsungs/
gser kha tshang gis phyag len 'di las gzhan du byed pa la
bka' bkyon mdzad tshul gyi lo rgyus kyang gsungs so/
/zhes klu'i bum gter gyi lag len rin chen bum bzang zhes
bya ba 'di yang dpag par dka' ba i spyod pa rgya mtsho la dbang
'byor pa'i bdag nyid chen po bka' drin zla med rdo rje 'chang
dngos ratna dhwa dza'i zhal snga nas kyis dgyes bzhin stsal
ba itar/ dge slong shes rab rgya mtshos bris pa bstan 'gro'i
phan bde'i gsos su smin par syur cig/

Mandala descriptions: A-khu-ching
1/gshed amar lha bcu gsum pa ni/ de yang phyi rol tu dur
khrod chen po brgyad kyis yongs su bskor ba'i (chos 'byung
yod) bsrung ba'i 'khor lo me ri dang bcas pa'i dbus su sna
tshogs padma la gnas pa'i sna tshogs rdo rje'i lte bar gzhal
yas khang gru bzhi sgo bzhi rgyan rta babs la sogs pa mtshan
nyid thams cad yongs su rdzogs pa'i dbus su bcom ldan 'das
gshin rje gshed amar po yab yum shar du gti mug gshin rje
gshed yab yum/ lhor ser sna gshin rje gshed yab yum/ nub tu
'dod chags gshin rje gshed yab yum/ byang du phrag dog gshin
rje gshed yab yüm/ grwa bzhir bum pa la gnas pa'i thod pa
bzhi/ shar sgor ya ma rā dzā/ (f. 57r) lho sgor ya me do ru/
nub sgor ya da yo ni/ byang sgor yakşe yatstsha ste gshin
rje gshed dmar po lha bcu gsum gyi rten dang brten pa'i dkyil

31/me ltar 'bar ba phrin las kyi dkyil 'khor ni de yang
phyi rol tu bsrung ba'i 'khor lo x rdzogs pa'i nang du khor
lo rtsibs bcu gnyis pa'i lte bar khro bo me itar 'bar ba/
phyogs kyi rtsibs bzhir/ khro bo khams gsum rnam rgyal/'jig
rten gsum 'dul/ 'jig rten gsum snang/ ta kki rā dzā/ de'i g.yas
kyi rtibs la bdud rtsi 'khyil ba/ rta mgrin/ stobs pa che/ mi
g.yo ba/ g.yon gyi rtsibs la/ dus kyi srin mo las kyi srin mo/
don gyi srin mo thabs kyi srin mo/ sgo bzhir/ dus kyi lcags
kyu ma/ dus kyi zhags pa ma/ dus kyi lcags sgrog ma/ dus kyi
dril bu ma ste me ltar 'bar ba 'phrin las kyi dkyil 'khor lha
bcu bdun gyi rten Xmdzod/ (f. 63v)
32/phyag na rdo rje rgyal chen bzhi sogs kyis bskor ba ni/
de yang phyi rol tu bsrung ba'i 'khor lo x rdzogs pa'i nang
du 'khor lo rtsibs bcu pa'i dbus su padma 'dab bzhi'i lte bar
phyag na rdo rje/ 'dab ma bzhi la yul 'khor srung/ 'phags skyes
po/ mig mi bzang/ lus ngan po rnams dang/ 'khor lo rtsibs bcu
la brgya byin/ me lha/ gshin rje/ srin po chu lha/ rlung lha/
gnod sbyin/ dbang ldan/, tshangs pad sa bdag ste phyogs skyong
bcu/ shar lhor sgeg mo/ lho nub tu phreng ba ma/ nub byang du
glu ma/ byang shar du gar ma/ shar sgor rdo rje lcags kyu/
lho sgor rdo rje zhags pa/ nub sgor rdo rje lcags sgrog/ byang
sgor rdo rje dril bu ste phyag na rdo rje rgyal chen bzhi sogs
kyis bskor ba lha nyer gsum gyi rten x mdzod/
33/phyag rdor gza' brgyad sogs kyis bskor ba ni/ de yang
phyi rol tu bsrung ba'i 'khor lo x dbus su phyag na rdo rje/
shar du zla ba/ shar lhor nyi ma/ lhor spen pa/ lhor nub tu
rā hu la/ nub tu dmag dpon/ nub byang du pa sangs/ byang du
phur bu/ byang shar du lag pa/ de'i phyi rol gyi shar du smin
drug/ snar ma/ mgo/ lag/ nabs so/ rgyal) skag/ lhor rta chen/
rta chung/ khra/ bya ma/ bya'u/ sa ri/ nub tu lag sor/ gdu bu/
sog pa/ bre phul/ gro zhun/ byi zhun/ byang du mon gre/ mon
gru/ khrums/ khrums smad/ nam gru/ tha skar/ bra nye/ grwa bzhir
sgeg sogs bzhi dang/ sgo bzhir rdo rje lcags kyu sogs bzhi ste
phyag na rdo rje la gza' brgyad sogs (f. 64r) kyis bskor ba lha
zhe Inga'i rten x mdzod/
34/phyag rdor klu brgyad kyis bskor ba ni/ de yang phyi rol
tu bsrung ba'i 'khor lo x dbus su dpal phyag na rdo rjel shar
du mtha' yas/ lhor 'jog po/ nub tu stobs rgyu) byang du rigs
ldan) shar lhor nor rgyas/ lho nub tu dung skyong/ nub byang
du padma/ byang shar du chu lha/ shar sgor rgyal rigs dkar po/

Mandala descriptions: A-khu-ching
kyi ngo bo khro bo hüm mdząd la rdo rje chos sogs kyi ngo bo
khro bo bzhis bskor ba/ byang du don grub kyi ngo bo khro bo
hūm mdzad la rdo rje las sogs kyi ngo bo khro bo bzhis bskor
ba/ grwa bzhir sgeg sogs bzhi dang/ phyi rol gyi khyam du
byams pa la sogs pa'i bskal bzang gi sems dpa" bcu drug/ de'i
mtshams bzhir bdug spos ma sogs bzhi dang/ sgo (f. 64v) bzhir
lcags kyu ma sogs bzhi ste khro bo khams gsum rnam rgyal lha
nga bdungyi rten x mdzod
36/'gro 'dul ni/ de yang phyi rol tu bsrung ba'i 'khor lo
x rdzogs pa rim pa gnyis su yod pa'i nang ma'i dbus su 'gro
ba 'dul bal shar du rdo rje sems ma/ lhor rin chen sems ma/
nub tu padma'i sems ma/ byang du las kyi sems ma/ shar lhor
spyan ma/ lho nub tu mā ma kí/ nub byang du gos dkar mo/ byang
shar du sgrol ma/ shar gyi ling tsher mi bskyod pa dang/ de'i
phyogs bzhir rdo rje sems dpa' sogs bzhi/ lhor rin 'byung
dang/ de'i phyogs bzhir rdo rje rin chen sogs/ nub tu snang ba
mtha' yas dang/ de'i phyogs bzhir rdo rje chos sogs bzhi/ byang
du don grub dang/ de'i phyogs bzhir rdo rje las sogs bzhi/ grwa
bzhir sgeg mo/ phreng ba ma/ glu ma/ gar ma/ khyams kyi mtshams
bzhir bdug spos ma/ me tog ma/ mar me ma/ dri chab ma/ sgo
sbrags kyi khyams la byams pa la sogs pa'i sems dpa' bcu drug/
grwa bzhir bdug spos ma sogs bzhi dang/ sgo bzhir lcags kyu ma
sogs bzhi ste 'gro ba 'dul ba lha re goig gi X mdzod
37/don thams cad grub pa ni/ de yang phyi rol tu bsrung
ba'i 'khor lo x rdzogs pa'i dkyil 'khor rim pa gnyis su yod
pa'i nang ma'i dbus su don yod grub pa/ shar du rdo rje sems
ma/ lhor rin chen sems ma/ nub tu padma'i sems ma/ byang du
las kyi sems ma/ shar gyi re mig tu don grub mi bskyod pa la
rdo rje sems dpa' sogs (f. 65r) bzhis bskor bad lhor don grub
rin 'byung la rdo rje rin chen sogs bzhis bskor bad nub tu
don grub snang mtha' la rdo rje chos sogs bzhis bskor ba/ byang
du don grub don yod grub pa la rdo rje las sogs bzhis bskor ba?

bdug spos ma sogs bzhi/ sgo sbrags kyi khyams su bskal bzang
gi sems dpa' bcu drug dang/ de'i grwa bzhir bdug spos ma sogs

cad grub pa lha nga bdun gyi x mdzod/

A-khu-ching on the Rdo rie 'phreng ba: Bibliography
Nyer mkho'i zin tho chu thigs phreng ba
Author: A-khu-ching Shes-rab-rgya-mtsho, 1803-1875.
Part 13 of Volume 7 (Ja) of the Lhasa Zhol New Printery edition
of the Gsung 'bum.
ff. llr-
/sa (f. llr) bzang 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros kyis mdzad
pa'i phreng ba dang kri ya sbrags pa'i mngon dkyil gyi lhan thabs/

dpe 'khrul med dngos grub gter mdzod/ 'phags sde lo tsā ba chab
mdo rje drung sngags rams pa dge 'dun bkra shis kyis mdzad pa'i
'phreng ba'i ngag don goal bại sgron me/ skyid shod zhabs drung
gis phreng ba gnyis kyi ngag 'don gyi rim pa khrigs su bsdebs pa
mthong bas don 'grub/ 1cangs skya ngag dbang chos ldan gyis mdzad
pa'i 'phreng ba kri ya'i dkyil "khor zhe lnga'i mngon dkyil gyi
cho ga bsgrigs blo gsal mgui rgyan nor bu'i 'phreng ba/ phreng
ba gnyis kyi mtha' apyod rig pa'i 'phrul gyi ide mig/ thar rtse
nam mkha' d pal bzang gi 'phreng ba dang kri ya sbrags pa'i sgrub
dkyil mdzes rgyan/ pan chen thams cad mkhyen pa blo bzang chos
kyi rgyal mtshan gyi rdzogs 'phreng lhan thabs/ bsam sgang pa ngag
dbang rdo rje 'dzin pa akon mchog rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa'i
dbang chog gi ngag 'don/

Rdo rje phreng ba: History
A-khu-ching Shes-rab-rgya-mtsho: Phreng ba'i dbang bshad zin
tho gsang chen gnad kyi sgron me. Part 1 of Volume 4 (Nga) of
the Lhasa New Zhol Printery edition of the gsung-'bum.
.../dbang bskur lag tu len tshul gyi dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga
mang yang gtso bo ni dkyil chog rdo rje phreng ba ste/ 'di
mdzad pa po'i che ba ni/ slob dpon a bha ya ka ra gupta zhes
pa bod skad du 'jigs med 'byung gnas sbas pa zhes rgya gar shar
phyogs singga la'i rgyal rigs su sku 'khrungs/ gzhon nu i dus nas
ma ga dhar rig pa'i gnas mtha' (f. 3r) dag la sbyangs pas gnas
Inga yongs rdzo gs kyi pandi ta chen por gyur/ rdo rje gdan gyi
rgyal po shing stan can gyis intra u la zhes pa'i sa gzhi phul
bar gtsug lag khang brtsigs/ nyin zhag gcig la thun gsum du byas
pa'ithun gcig la bs tan bcos rtsom/ thun gcig la chos 'chad/ thun
gcig la ting nge 'dzin la mnyam par 'jog cing bzhugs/ de l'ta bu'i
dus skabs cig na bud med cig gis sha chang phul te 'di zos shing
'thung na don chen po 'grub par 'gyur ro zer ba la bdag dge slong
yin pas mi rung dgongs nas ma bzhes/ bud med song ba'i rjes su
btsal kyang ma rnyed/ rkang rjes su me tog u dum ba ra skyes pa
gzigs nas rdo rje rnal 'byor ma yin par shes te gsol ba yun ring
du btab pas zhai mngon sum du gzigs/
rgyud sde bzhi'i lha tshogs thams cad kyi dbang bskur zhing
byin gyis brlabs/ khyad par du rje btsun rdo rje mal 'byor mas
khyod kyis rgyud sde bzhi'i dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi sgrub thabs
dang dbang bskur ba'i cho ga sogs bstan bcos mang po byas na
sngar nga i ngag bcag pa'i sdig pa 'dag cing/ bar dor mchog gi
dngos grub 'grub ces lung bstan pas/ sampu ta'i 'grel ba man ngag
snye ma sangs rgyas thod pa'i rgyud tik jigs med gzhung grel
sogs bstan boos 'bum phrag gcig mdzad par grags
khyad par dkyil 'khor gyi lha tshogs mang po'i sgrub thabs
phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa rnal 'byor rdzogs phreng/ dbang bskur
ba'i phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa dkyil chog rdo rie phreng ba
de dag gi bsnyen pa'i kha skong sbyin sreg ston pa 'od snye ste
de gsum PHRENG BA (f. 3v) SKOR GSUM du grags/ de i dbang rgyun
pandi ta dge ba'i 'byung gnas/ dpe med bsrung ba/ rnam bshad lha
sogs la rim par brgyud de 'phags yul du rgya cher dar/
dbang rgyun bod gangs can gyi ljongs su spel ba po kha che'i
pandi ta shākya shri yin la/ des rgya gar gyi pandi ta bi khyā
ta de ba dang/ shākya rakşi ta gnyis la dbang rdzogs par zhus te
mnga' ris su phreng ba'i dbang thams cad bskur/
slar yang slob dpon bhu mi shri sogs la tshar gcig dang/
phyis su sne'u rdzong du dkyil 'khor nyer brgyad du bsdus pa'i
dbang bskur yang mdzad/ de ltar pan chen shakya shri nas brgyud
du bod du ches cher dar ba byung phreng ba'i dbang zhe gnyis yod
kyang deng sang zhe Inga mdzad pa kri ya nas bde legs su byed pa'i
dkyil 'khor gsum bsnan pa yin la/ de yang kri ya sa mu tstska'am
bya ba bsdus pa ni darpā na a tsa rya ste pandi ta 'gro ba'i me
long zhes pa rje btsun rdo rje rnal 'byor mas rjes su bzung ste
'chi med tshe'i rig 'dzin brnyes pas tshems lan nyi shu brjes par
grags pa des mdzad
kri ya nas dkyil 'khor zhe Inga bshad pas zhe gnyis rdor
phreng dang mi 'dra ba med pas des 'thus pa byas te bde legs su
byed pa'i dkyil 'khor gsum bsnan pa yin/ kri ya'i lo rgyus kyi
dbang du byas na/ sa bzang 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros kyis bal
yul du byon te pandi ta ma hā bo dhi la kri ya'i dbang rdzogs
par zhus te rdor phreng dang kri ya sbrags pa'i sgrub dkyil gyi
ihan thabs mdzad cing/ dbang gi chu bo gnyis 'dres su gyur pa de
nas bzung ste bdag gi drin can rtsa ba'i bla ma'i bar du brgyud
pa bar ma chad cing/ byin (f. 4r) rlabs kyi ngad ma yal bar byung
ba de lta bu'i dbang bskur gsan pa la sta gon dang dngos gzhi



.

Mi tra brgya rtsa: History
A-khu-ching Shes-rab-rgya-mtsho: Mi tra'i dbang bshad zin tho
mnam grol bdud rtsi'i snye ma. Part 2 of Volume 4 (Ngay of the
Lhasa New Zhol Printery edition of the gsung-'bum.
.../'dir rgyal ba kun gyi thugs rje'i bdag nyid 'phags mchog
phyag na padmas rjes su bzung ste phyag rgya chen po mchog gi dros
grub brnyes pa/ zung 'jug nor buli za ma tog/ ngo mtshar ba'i rnam
thar bco brgyad dang idan pa'i grub pa'i 'khor los bsgyur ba/ rnal
'byor gyi dbang phyug mi tra dzo ki'am mtshan gzhan dpal ldan chos
kyi bshes gnyen gyis 'phags pa'i bkas gnang ba stsal ba la brten
nas/ phyi rabs kyi gdui bya mnams la phan pa'i phyir thugs bcud
zab mo phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa/ gsang chen bstan pa'i nying
khu MI TRA BRGYA RTSAr grags pa'i abang gi rim pa mnams 'bul bar
byed pa la/ thog mar gshin rje gshed dmar po'i abang bskur ba la
rten 'brel dang dgos pa khyad par can yod pas/ dam pa gong ma rnams
kyi phyag len la'ang de ltar mdzad kyi yod gsungs/
rgyal ba rgya mtsho'i dbang gi nyin spyi bshad la/ dus gsum
rgyal ba thams cad kyi dmigs pa med pa'i snying rje'i rang gzugs
thugs rje'i gter chen mgon po spyan ras gzigs zhes rgyal sras dpa'
bo kun gyi nang nas snying rje'i gter du bsngags shing/ khyad par
byang phyogs kha ba can gyi ijongs 'di ston pa shākya'i rgyal po
nyid kyis angos kyi 'dul zhing du ma gyur pa mgon po 'di la ched
du gtad pa bzhin phyag mtshan du bzhes te sgo mtha' dag nas skyong
bar mdzad pas rang cag rnams kyi lha skal dang/ phyogs bcu'i rgyal
ba (f. 4r) sras dang bcas pa bsnyen bkur ba las 'di nyid kyi
smýung gnas byas pas bskal pa du ma'i 'khor ba phyir bsnyii ba
dang/ bsam pa rnam par dag pas gzugs sngags bzlas pas phan yon
mtha' yas pa 'byung tshul tshad mar gyur pa'i mdo rgyud du ma nas
yang yang gsungs pa ltar yin zhing/ gsang ba gsum gyi zlos gar
mtha' yas pas gdul bya so so'i skal ba dang 'tshams par skuli bkod
pa mi 'dra ba mtha' yas pa yod pas/ dam pa gong ma rnams la brgyud
pa'i lugs srol yang de snyed yod pa dge slong ma dpal mo nas
brgyud pa DPAL MO'I LUGS/ chos rgyal srong btsan sgam po nas
brgyud pa RGYAL PO'I LUGS/ byang sems zla ba rgyal mtshan las
brgyud pa ZLA RGYAL LUGS/ la stod dmar po nas brgyud pa LA STOD
LUGS/ gnyan tshem bu ba las brgyud pa TSHEM BU DMAR KĀRID/ grub
thob skyer sgang pa las brgyud pa SÃYER SGANG LUGS sogs mang du
yod pa las/ skabs su babs pa grub chen mi tra dzo ki nas brgyud
pa'i bla med lugs kyi 'phags mchog spyan ras gzigs sku mdog dkar
po zhal gcig phyag gnyis yum bcas/ 'khor mkha' 'gro ma bzhi dang/
khro bo bzhis bskor ba lha dgu ma 'di'i sngags la yang dag mi dag
sna tshogs zhig yod pa rgyal dbang bskal bzang rgya mtshos dag
ther mdzad de/ om ma pi padme hüm zhes pa gtso bo'i sngags/
dhu ma gha ye yum gyi sngags/ ha ri ni sa mkha' 'gro bzhi dang/
ra tsa hrih ya khro bo bzhi'i sa bon gyi sngags yin pas/ de yongs
rdzogs la bsnyen pa byas pas gtso 'khor yongs rdzogs kyi bsnyen
pa'i go chod la/ ma pi rkyang pas (f. 4v) kyang chog pas ma ni
mtha' gcig tu bya rgyud kyi lugs su byas nas bgrang dgos pa'i
nges pa med par cho ga phyag len thams cad bla med Itar byas te
lha 'di lta bu dang 'brel bar bzlas na mchog tu gyur pa yin gsungs/



Gtor ma brgya rtsa
A-khu-ching Shes-rab-rgya-mtsho, 1803-1875: Gtor ma brgya rtsa'i
khrid kyi bried byang bdud rtsi'i dga' ston. Part 23 of Volume
3 (Ga) of the Lhasa New Zhol Printery edition of the gsung-'bum.
/na mo gu ru buddha bo dhi satwe bhyah/
/thugs rje'i gter chen phyag na padmo dang/
Zabyer med bla ma'i zhabs la gus btud nas/
Zrlabs chen bsod nams sdud pa'i thabs kyi mchog/
7tshogs gsog brgya rtsa'i zhal gdams dang 'dir spel/
7'dir bya sla la don che zhing tshegs chung ba tshogs
gsog pa'i thabs dang 'phrul 'degs che ba'i gdams pa GTOR MA
BRGYA RTSA zhes grags pa 'di'i khungs ni/ bdud rtsi 'byung ba'i
gzungs dang/. yi dwags kha la me 'bar ma la skyabs mdzad pa'i
gzungs dang/ kha 'bar ma dbugs dbyung ba'i gzungs sogs la brten
zhing/ kha 'bar ma'i idos chog kyang gzungs phyi ma gnyis la
khungs bcol ba yin/ brgya rtsa'i gdams pa mnyam med jo bo chen
pos bod du gnang pas bka' gdams kyi dam pa gong ma mang pos
thugs nyams su bzhes shing/ snar thang brgya rtsa'i nang du'ang
yod/ blo sbyong las 'byung ba'i sbyor ba bzhi sogs rang shugs
kyis chang ba'i tshogs gsog thabs zla med yin pas grub mtha
ris med la dar so che/ de'ang nyams len thams cad tshogs bsags
sgrib sbyangs la 'du/ yon tan gang don du gnyer kyang de'i rgyur
tshogs bsags dgos pa rgyu dge sdig las 'bras bu bde sdug 'byung
ba'i rtags kyis 'grub/ tshogs tsam gyis mi chog bar 'gal rkyen
sgrib pa sbyong ba'i gnad tshang dgos/ tshogs gnyis las dang
pos gzugs sku (f. lv) dang/ gnyis pas dag pa gnyis ldan gyi chos
sku grub pas bsod nams kyi tshogs yon tan sgrub byed dang/ ye
shes kyi tshogs sgrib pa slong byed yin/ tshogs bsags sgrib
sbyong gtso cher sems steng nas byung dgos kyang lag len du
'debs tshul gyi thabs khyad 'phags brgya rtsar grags pa 'di
gtso bor tshogs bsags dang/ zhar la sgrib sbyong gi gnad mang
po tshang pa de bzhin gshegs pa bzhi'i mtshan gyi phan yon Ita
bus kyang shes gsungs/
de yang brgya rtsa gtong ba'i rten gyi gang zag dge bsnyen
yan chad kyi sdom ldan byung na gzhung nas bshad pa ltar yin
pas legs/ gzhan gyis 'bul mi rung ba min/ 'on kyang lha'i mnal
'byor gyi sgo nas gtor ma bsangs sbyangs bskyed de 'bul ba la
bya rgyud thugs rje chen po'i dbang ita bu zhig thob pa dgos/
gnas mchod sbyin lugs la rang rang gi gnas su phar btang bas
sa khad yang dog la khyad par cher med kyang/ iha'i d
rnam pa ma byas par mgron rang rang gi gzugs su spyan 'dren pa'i
lugs la dbang che ba 'ga' zhig gi nye 'khor du dbang chung ba
mams 'ong mi nus pas sa khad yangs par byas na de dag la phan
gdags pa'i dgos pa yod/phar bsngos kyang tshur 'ong ba mang
bas sa khad yangs pa sogs 'grig na legs/ gnas nges med du btang
na mgron mngon shes med pa 'ga' zhig gtor ma don du (f. 2r)
gnyer nas 'ong kyang sbyin pa po ma rnyed par gtor ma ma thob
pa'i lo rgyus yod pas gnas nges can 'grig na legs/ dus tshod
snga dro mar mgron phal cher gyis zas tshol ba'i dus yin pas
de 'i tshe 'bul ba byung na legs/ zas zos pas lus kyi gzi mdangs
rgyas nas 'byung po'i rigs phra mo 'ga' zhig nye 'khor du 'ong
mi nus pa srid pas nang snga mo ito stong la gtong thub na legs
pa klong rdol bla ma las thos zhes rgyal mkhan chen rin po ches
gsungs/
nye 'khor du mtshon cha dang/ lcags dang/ gzugs brnyan
'char ba'i rigs bzhag na las dbang gis snang ba sna tshogs 'chan
bas 'gyod pa dang skrag nas 'ong mi nus pa mang bas de 'dra'i
rigs sbed/ zas kyi dri bro ba'i sa nas btang na yi dwags 'jur
'gag gis chu sbyin mi thob pas tha na sen mo'i bar du yang zas
kyi dri med pa byed/ nye 'khor du zas sna tshogs bzhag na yi



A-khu-ching on Medicine
'Dul ba dang sngags kyi tshig bkra sogs
ff. 24r et ff.
Part 10 of volume Ja of the Gsung 'bum of A-khu-ching Shes-rab-rgya-
mtsho, 1803-1875, in the Lhasa New Zhol printery edition.
/rgya gar skad du/ a mrI ta hri da ya angga aşta gu hya u pa
de sha tantra na ma/ bod skad du/ bdud rtsi snying po yan lag brgyad
pa gsang ba man ngag gi rgyud (f. 24r) ces bya ba/ /zhes pa nas/
bdud rtsi snying po yan lag brgyad pa gsang ba man ngag gi rgyud
ces bya ba sangs rgyas sman gyi bla bai dūrya 'od kyi rgyal po'i
byin rlabs las sprul pa'i ston pa drang srong rig pa'i ye shes
dang drang srong yid las skyes kyis zhus lan du mdzad pa gso
dpyad kun gyi rgyal po zhes bya ba rdzogs so/ /zhes pa'i bar gyi
gzhung 'di gang las 'phros na/ 'dul ba sman gyi gzhi las/
sman ni rjes su gnang ba dang/
/tshil dang g.yan pa mig sman dang/
/smyon pa dang ni pi linda/
nam giu dang ni skyur khu'o/ /zhes pa'i sdoms kyis bsdus
pa'i gzhung 'di las 'phros par thal/ 'phros tshul gzhung 'di'i
skabs su gang gso bar bya ba lus dang nad kyi rang bzhin/ gang,
gis gso bar byed pa'i sman đpyad zas spyod/ des ji ltar gso ba'i
thabs kyi tshul gleng gzhi dang sbyar nas bstan tshul de ji lta
bu yin zhe na/ de'i lan du gso ba rig pa thams cad kyi don gyi
gnad 'gag bsdus te bshad pa sa bon ita bu rtsa ba'i rgyud/ de'i
don rgyas par bshad pa yal 'dab lta bu bshad pa'i rgyud man ngag
lag len gyi sgo nas gtan la 'bebs pa me tog lta bu man ngag gi
rgvud zab gnad snying por dril ba 'bras bulta bu phyi ma'i rgyud
bzhis 'chad pa la drangs ma thag pa'i gzhung 'di byung ya yin
pa'i phyir/ pra dznyā sā ga ra li khi tam/

A-khu-ching's Miscellaneous notes
Mdo phyogs kyi gsung thor 'ga' zhig
ff. 27
Author: A-khu-ching Shes-rab-rgya-mtsho, 1803-1875
Part 8 of vol. Ja of the Gsung 'bum in the Lhasa Zhol New Printery
edition.
MON SPA GRO'I RDOR GCOD ces pa yul der rdor good ma dag pa
mang po yod pa/ dag po gcig min pa med pas thams cad bsdur te dag
pa gcig pu phyin chad 'dris med par byas te/ mi dag pa rnams mthun
pas 'di mams dag ces bshad pa bzhin du mis bshad pa la chag bzhag
med/ 'jig rten pa rnams kyis de la ngan lab ns de rnams dang mi
mthun par song na de chos dang mthun pa'i rtags yin zhes bshad
mkhan yod gsungs/
/SHWA PO SGANG PA rang stong nyid la mnyam par bzhag pa zhig
yin pas g.yas g.yon chu log gis bshig ste khong bzhugs sa la sgang
dod pa la zer/ shwa 'od ni chu log gi ming yin gsungs/
/DWAGS PO LHA RJE'i slob ma phag mo gru pa/ de'i slob ma
gtsang pa rgya ras/ de'i brgyud 'dzin mnams la 'brug pa byung/
sa skya ba dgon pa'i ming/
Ici 'dra yod na'ang, chags zhen med/
med na'ang (f. llr) mi dga' ba med par ro mnyam/ rtsam pa
pag khug gang las med pa dang/ rtsam pa sgam gang yod pa gnyis
las sgam gang yod pa la sdug che/ lan 'dus gcig yod na de kha
rgyab byed mi thub par bsags te kha rgyab gzhan nas btsal nas lan
'dus bou 'go tshang/ de yang kha rgyab byed mi thub par bsags
nas rgya la sogs pa byung na yang des kha rgyab byed mi thub chos
byed mi thub par bsags nas bzhag ste bltas bsdad pa dang/ pha ri'i
ri kun gser yin bsam nas bltas_bsdad pa gnyis la khyad par spu
tsam yang med pas dgos pa cung zad kyang med gsungs/

Skyes rabs so bzhi pa
'Jam mgon sde khri rin po che'i drung du gsan pa'i skyes rabs so
bzhi pa'i bshad pa'i zin bris
ff. 22
Author: A-khu-ching Shes-rab-rgya-mtsho, 1803-1875
Part 12 of Vol. 5 (ca) of the Lha-sa Zhol New Printery edition of
the Gsung 'bum.
.../me bya (1837) zla 1 tshes 8 kyi gsung chos la/ khams gsum bla
ma tsong kha pa chen po'i zhal nas/
dal ba'i rten 'di yid bzhin nor las lhag/ /ces pa nas/
thar 'dod khyed kyang de bzhin bskyang (f. lv) 'tshal' 10)
zhes khams gsum bla ma rang nyid kyis thugs nyams su ji ltar bstar
ba'i tshul rang cag mams la 'doms par mdzad pa de'i tshe na/
dal 'byor tshang ba'i rten 'di yid bzhin gyi nor bu rin po che
ltar myed par dka'zhing/ de ltar myed aka' ba tsam du ma zad
snyigs dus kyi tshe thung goig la rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi go
'phang yang sgrub tu yod pas don che/...
de ang sngon gyi dam pa mnams kyis dus chen spyi dang/ khyad
par chos 'phrul smon lam gyi skabs skyes rabs 'chad pa'i srol
btsugs pa dus khyad par can la smon lam gang btab brgya stong 'bum
'gyur du 'gro bas rgyal ba'i sras kyi spyod pa skye bo mnams kyi
khong du chud par byas nas dad pa bskyed de de la slob 'dod thang
gcig skyes pa tshun chad dus gzhan du lo bskal pa'i bar bsam bsam
pa las gyur khyad che ba dang/ 'chad tshul mdzad pa po'i che ba/
chos kyi che ba sogs/ byang chub lam gyi rim pa'i sa bcad kyi
khungs ci lta ba bzhin skyes rabs 'chad pa'i thog mar yang mdzad
pa po'i che ba 'chad pas 'di mdzad pa po/ SLOB DPON DPA' BO ni/
ston pa bcom ldan 'das kyis 'jam dpal rtsa ba'i rgyud du/
dge slong mang du thos pa ni/ /zhes sogs skyes pa'i rabs
kyi tshul las brtsams te bston pa byed par lung bstan ma khol
lam rta dbyangs (f. 3v) zhes bya ba 'di nyid sngon ston pa 'od
ma'i tshal du 'khor mang po la chos ston pa'i skabs nam mkha' nas
bya rog cig gis bya thal btang pa abu la bab pa 'khor rnams kyis
rgyu mtshan zhus pas/ ma 'ongs pa na mu stegs kyi pandi ta thub
aka' bar 'gyur zhes lung bstan pas 'khor de'i nang nas byang chub
sems dpa' lag na padmo zhes bya ba stan las langs te bdag gis der
skye ba blang ba nas mu stegs de sangs rgyas kyi bstan par gzud
par bya'o zhes smon lam btab pa bzhin sing ga la'i gling gi rgyal
po'i sras su 'khrungs/ mgon po klu sgrub las rab tu byung stel
sde snod gsum la mkhas par sbyangs pa'i mtshan 'phags pa lha zhes
grags/ de dang dus mtshungs par sngar gyi bya rog de'ang rgya gar
shar phyogs mu stegs bram ze'i rigs su skyes/ phyi pa'i gzhung la
mkhas par sbyangs/ yul de'i nang pa'i pandi ta mams dang bstan
pa rgyal du btsugs nas brtsad pas kun pham/ma de'i nang pa la dad
pas thabs shig byed pa las 'os med/ snyam nas sangs rgyas kyi
bstan pa rta'i lus tsam pa la rgya gar shar lho na rta'i rna ba
tsam las med pas rgyal ba'i ming mi thob/ yul dbus na pandi ta
mang bas der song na legs zer ba bzhin der 'ongs pa na dbang phyug
sgrub ste phyogs ram par. rgyal ba'i dngos grub blangs yod pas yul
dbus kyi pandi ta mnams kyang sems khong du tshud/ klu sgrub yab
sras bzhugs pa'i drung du 'phrin gyi yi ge bya rog la bskur bas
slob dpon 'phags pa lha phebs nas rtsod pas pham par byas kyang/
pandi ta chen po'i (f. 4r) snyem pa'i dbang gis nang pa'i bstan
pa la 'jug tu ma 'dod pa na sde snod mang po bzhugs pa'i gtsug lag
khang đu bzhag pas'jam apal rtsa rgyuu kyi lung de yin pa 'dra/
gang ltar rang nyid lung bstan pa'i mdo mthong ste ston pa
la snying thag pa nas gus pa rmad du byung ba 'khrungs te sngar
ston pa dang bstan par rma byung ba'i nyes pa sbyangs phyir skyes
rabs 'di la sogs pa md zad/ des na 'di 'chad pa la da res rten
'brel gyis dbu nas zhu na/ klad kyi don/ gzhung gi don/ mjug gi
don gsum/
dang po la mtshan don dang/ 'gyur phyag gnyis las/ dang po

A-khu-ching on the Skyes rabs so bzhi pa
ni/ rgya gar na skad rigs bzhi las sang ki ri ta'i skad du/ dza
ta sogs bod skad du skyes rabs kyi rgyud del sngon stag mor lus
sbyin pa nas bya shing rta mor gyur nas seng ge'i gre ba nas rus pa
zug pa bton pa'i skyes rabs kyi bar tha mal ba mams dang mam pa
mthun pa dang/ thams cad rang rang dang skal ba 'tshams par snang
ba'i sgo nas thabs sna tshogs kyis rang gi chos la gzung rung du
byas pa de dag gi tshe pha rol du phyin pa drug las brtsams pa'i
spyod pa ji snyed cig mdzad pa'i gtam ni rabs dang/ stag mor lus
sbyin pa nas bya shing rta mo'i bar gyi skyes rabs go rim thar
chags su yod pas rgyud de/ rgyud ni rgyun chags pa la 'jug pas
phreng ba'i ming gis kyang btags/ mtshan 'dogs lugs kyi steng nas
brjod bya'i khog shes rgyu yod dgos pas/ mtshan 'dogs lugs la dgos
pa yod pa mngon rtogs rgyan Ita bu 'di la brten nas sher mdo'i don
ma rtogs pa rtogs lugs kyi gnad khyad par can zhig dang/ de'i
gnad gsal bar (f. 4v) 'char rgyu zhig yod par go ba itar/ 'dir
yang stag mor lus sbyin pa nas bya shing rta mo'i bar gyi gtam
rgyud mnams ge sar gyi sgrung ltar ma yin par pha rol tu phyin
pa drug las brtsams te gsungs pas rgyal sras kyi spyod pa la slob
na skyes rabs nas 'byung ba itar slob dgos snyam pa dang/ rang
slob mi nus snyam du dpa' zhum pa La ston pa sngon rten dman par
skyes kyang snying stobs khyad par 'phags pas spyod pa rlabs chen
po de ita bu grub na/ rang re dal 'byor tshang ba'i mi'i lus rten
thob ste/ blang dor gyi mam bzhag shes pa de Itar 'bad pas bslab
na go 'phang mchog de 'dra ba ci'i phyir mi 'grub snyam du rjes
su slobº 'dod kyis 'jug pa las/ sngon skyes rabs 'khrungs rabs kyi
lo rgyus ge sar gyi sgring ltar dpa' thul 'di zhes bya ba'i dgra
'dul gnyen skyong 'thab rtsod 'khrugs long sogs ji snyed cig byas
pa'i gtam ltar nyan pas gnad du ma song ba yin pas sems steng du
blangs te chos nas ci skad gsungs pa ltar rang sems la 'grub pa
dgos/ bam po ni gzhúng gi cha sil bu mang po phyogs goig du bsdoms
pa gzhung tshan mi 'chug pa'i ched mdzad de/ bam po kha mar Ita
zhes gzhung tshan de dang de'i 'go dang/ le'u kha yar Ita zhes
dper na mam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi skabs te dang polo/
/zhes pa lta bu mjug du yod/ 'gyur mthar phyin pa'i ched ngag gi
dbang phyug la phyag 'tshal ba ni lo tsā bas 'dod pa'i lha la
phyag byas pa yin par gsungs 'dug/
Zde nas shis brjod phyag bya ngo bo ni/
/nges par bstan pa'ang de yi sgo/ /zhes pa (f. 5r) itar ngo
bo nges bstan gyis 'chad par/ dpal idan yon tan dam pas yongs
bzung bkra shis pa/ /zhes sogs te/...

A-khu-ching's Studies
Thog mtha' bar du dge ba'i dam pa'i chos kyi thob yig mdo sngags
zab rgyas bdud rtsi'i mtsho las skra rtses blangs pa'i chu thigs
Volume Cha in the Lhasa Zhol New Printery edition of his Gsung 'bum.
Author: A-khu-ching Shes-rab-rgya-mtsho, 1803-1875.
A-khu-ching's Teachers
...lam de nyams su blang ba'i 'bras bur che ba bzhi sogs 'byung
ba'i phyir/ de ltar 'ong ba'ang thos bsam dang dpyad sgom kho na la
rag las par rje bla mas lam rim che chung sogs su yang yang gsung
ba ltar lags kyang rang la ni thos pa tshol ba'i 'dun pa tsam yod
na'ang 'di snang gi g.yengs pa du mas mnar te smon pa'i yul du
gyur pas shin tu skyo/ 'on kyang skyabs mgon thams cad mkhyen cing
gzigs pa chen po rje btsun BLO BZANG THUB BSTAN 'JIGS MED RGYA
MTSXO'I SDE/ 'jam a pal dbyangs dngos DKON MCHOG BSTAN PA'I SGRON
ME/ Spyan ras gzigs abang MKHAN CHEN GRAGS PA RGYAL MTSHANX gsang
bdag grub pa'i dbang phyug SDE KHRI RIN PO CHE 'JAM DBYANGS THUB
BSTAN NYI MA/ bskal pa bye bar mgo la thod bzhin bkur kyang bka'
drin 'khor thabs dang bral ba 'jam dbyangs bla ma rdo rje 'chang
DKON MCHOG RGYAL MTSHAN sogs thub dbang rdo rje 'chang gis bdag
(f. 4r)nyid rjes su 'dzin phyir dngos su sprul pa'i mtshan ldan
dge ba'i bshes gnyen 'jam dpal dbyangs lta bu bcu phrag gsum du
nye ba'i zhabs la gtugs te yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas
nas bzung dam pa bar ma chad pa las brgyud pa'i dbang rjes gnang
lung khrid man ngag mi nyung tsam 'bad pas mnos pa rnams tshe rabs
phyi ma rnams su dam pa'i chos kyi snang ba khyad par can dang mi
bral bar smon pa'i phyir dang/ bstan rgyun dang/ gzhan dag la
yang cha shas phramo re yin kyang phan par gyur na ci ma rung
snyam du chos khungs btsun par bstan pa'i phyir mdzad pa po'i che
ba gsungs pa'i tshul dang mthun par 'god pa la/ rang lo bcu drug.
pa rab byung bcu bzhi pa'i bgrangs bya bcu gnyis pa sa stag(1818)
zla ba bcu pa'i tshes brgyad la dben gnas yid dga' chos 'azin bsam
gtan 'phel rgyas gling du 'phags pa'i gnas brtan chen po DKON MCHOG
DGE DÜN las skyabs 'gro rtsom byed du byas te tshangs spyod dge
bsnyen gyi sdom pa dang bar ma rab byung gi tshul khrims mnos te
rgyal ba'i bstan pa rin po che'i sgor zhugs pa'i skal bzang thob/
de'i lo phyi ma'i mnyan yod cho 'phrul mchod pa'i dus sten gyi
tshes bco Ingar gzims chung dge legs bde yangs su yongs rdzogs
bstan pa'i mnga' bdag 'dul ba 'dzin pa mtha' dag gi gtsug rgyan
'jam dpal dbyangs dngos DKON MCHOG BITAN PA'I SGRON ME'i zhabs
drung nas rab byung bskyar ma dang tshigs snga ma dge tshul gyi
sdom pa legs par nod de mkhan po rnam pa gnyis kas ming DKON MCHOG ordinat-
BSTAN 'DZIN zhes stsal/
ion name
rang lo nyer brgyad pa lcags stag (1830) sa ga zla ba'i tshes
brgyad la bla brang thub bstan pho trang gi gzims chung du stobs
(f. 4v) bcu mnga' ba shākya'i rgyal po dngos dang dbyer ma mchis
pa'i rje btsun bla ma dam pa don gyi slad du mtshan nas smos na
mkhan po 'dul ba rgya mtsho'i mnga' bdag thams cad mkhyen pa BLO
BZANG THUB BSTAN 'JIGS MED RGYA MTSHOs mkhan slob sbrags ma dang/
smra ba'i khyu mchog sgo me lha rams pa BLO BZANG CHOS 'DZIN gyis
gsang ston/ rdo rams pa DKON MCHOG SANGS RGYAS kyis dus go ba? KLU
SHOD PA BLO BZANG DKON MCHOG dang/ sngags rans på DKON MCHOG BSTAN
DAR gnyis kyis las kyi kha skong ba mdzad de dad pa'i dge 'dun
grangs tshang ba'i dbus su rab byung dge tshul bskyar sgrub thob
bslab gzhi yongs su rdzogs pa'i dge slong gi sdom pa legs par stsal
te ming SHES RAB RGYA MTSHO zhes gnang ngo/
final name
